et n’apresser mie ta main a tout le cautere, et soit li malaides sovins sor son dos;	 And do not press your hand on the entire cauterization, and let the patient be aware of his back.
et une autre maniere de cautere si est que tu eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners, si com nos l’avons mostreit en la dislocation de l’espaule;	 And another way of cautery is that you heat the cauter iron with two prongs, as shown in the dislocation of the shoulder.
et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	 And lift the iron that is near the mouse, where the pain of the patient comes towards the left side, and raise the elevations from which you heat the iron according to the length of the body, and the cauter iron according to the width of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII.	 After placing the two prongs heated together until the iron is pierced on the other side, then pull the cauter iron away, and in this way there will be four.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	 And if you wish to cauterize with all of the cautery using three prongs.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	 After treatment when he has had pus for long time, and it is worth applying the other remedies mentioned before.
de ydropisie	The translation for this line would be "of hydropisia." Hydropisia refers to a medical condition in which there is excessive accumulation of water or fluid in the body tissues, specifically in the abdominal cavity.
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	 Cautery is not effective against dropsy, except in the manner called "asclytes".
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis;	 When the treatment according to the methods that we have mentioned in divisions does not help, then it is necessary that you make four cauteries around the wound, one above the stomach, one above the liver, one above the mouse, two behind the back near the spine, and one at the site of pain.
et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	 And let the cautery be close to the swelling of the sore.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere;	 After open (the wound) for a long time and let it purge pus, but do not abandon the treatment of the patient after the cautery.
et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	 And healing will hasten, and the two intentions will be together with God's help.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit;	 The form of the cautery for the belly is the crucible that we have previously shown.
et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	 And for the back it should be olive-shaped, as described earlier.
de l’enfleure des piez	of the swelling on the feet
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire;	 When the feet are swollen in someone who is dropsical, and they are full of hot liquid, you should cauterize on the back of the foot between the little finger and the ring finger;
et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	 hold your hand with the cautery without turning it.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	 And do not go too deep, otherwise the citrine would be forceful; and make sure the cautery is in this shape:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire;	 After doing two cauteries on each leg at the point of the knife blade;
et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe;	 and let the cauterized area be long, one under the knee in front and the other outside, within the leg;
et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse;	 And let the cauteries heal over time on their own, for it heals them.
aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	 after the healing of other treatments that we have mentioned.
de la menoison	swelling
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures;	 When the abdominal distention comes from cold and moisture, as long as the digestive and restorative powers which are in the stomach and intestines are weakened and cannot be healed by means of treatments;
et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule;	 and you see the patient suffering greatly and of strong constitution, make a large cautery on the stomach as mentioned earlier, or stomach cauterization, around the stomach.
et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	 and three subtle cauteries around the navel, at every cautery joint, and two cauteries on the flanks.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et .i. cautere sus chaicun yle, et .ij. petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see the moisture abundant and the patient suffering, apply cautery on the joint, one cautery on each joint, and two small cauteries on the stomach in addition to the large one, because the cure is beneficial where there is good aid.
de la cure des emorroydes	of the cure for hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres:	 When hemorrhoids are deeply rooted, single or multiple, and are old, filled with large cold and moist corrupted humors, and have been treated as we have said in the previous section, and it does not help, then apply fire cauteries.
III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois;	 On the spine of the back, that which is completely dislocated under the occipital bone and moves triangularly, the fire cautery should be applied beneath the buttock.
et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile;	 If you suspect that the stomach is cooled and meat does not cook, and swelling of the face is seen, then the great fire cautery should be applied on the stomach as previously mentioned, and another one on the liver, and another one on the spleen with a full-length cautery.
et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	 And let the fire cautery remain open for a long time.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	 After healing the joint when it is healthy.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the charnositeit which is named "thelul"
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit;	 When you treat athlete's foot, if the fire cautery seems to be a razor, then heat it and place it on top of the athlete's foot so treated.
et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort;	 and let your hand be such that the cautery comes to the opening of the vein, so that it does not cut.
fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit;	 Do this once or twice, and if there is much athlete's foot, then cauterize each one as we have said.
aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez;	 After the cures of ointments are beneficial until they are healed.
et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	 And if you cauterize with a large cautery on scrofula (a chronic inflammatory disease), it will have more help.
de plaie mal curee	from an improperly treated wound
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	If the patient cannot bear incision or opening, which we will explain in its place, this disease comes that can only be healed by cauterization.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	 If any abscess comes, and it is swollen, rotten, and corrupted with moisture, you should probe the whole cavity with a subtle needle, and ensure that you know exactly how deep the hole goes.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing;	 After heating the cautery that seems like a razor, and pushing it into the fistula according to how much it was entered, start the cauterization until the body parts become burned and corrupted, once, or II or III times, according to the amount of soreness required.
et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	 And beware of burning the nerve that is within, and the great veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans;	 if the fistula goes to the body of the bladder and the intestines, beware of these places, and do not act carelessly except in a charcoal fire, and think that it is not useless.
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement;	 after curing the place until it is clean, and if the places are purulent and the matter has been removed for a long time, then know that the place is completely clean.
et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font;	 And if the tissues are not removed, know that the joint is broken, and the bone is corrupt.
et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	 And as one of these whom we will describe in his place.
de la maladie des reins	on the disease of the kidneys
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit;	 When cold pain comes at the joints and from large wind, and does not respond to female remedies, then you must make a fire cautery on both sides of the joints with the claw-shaped fire cautery as we have previously said.
et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	 And if we perform the cauterization in the middle, it will have three cauterizations in a row, and they will be more helpful.
de la vessie	of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce;	 When the bladder is soft and weak from cold and moisture, causing the patient to retain urine, then you make a cauterization on the outside of the bladder where the pubic hair begins, both on the right and left side, and each cauterization should be as long as one's thumb.
et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing;	 And make the fire cautery outside the back, where it is needed.
et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	 and let the fire cautery be attached in the shape mentioned above.
de la marris	of the anus
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde;	 When the matrix is cold and moist, it does not allow conception to take place, and the flowers are corrupt and their terms are delayed.
et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor:	 and when they come, there is great pain.
adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos;	 Then it is necessary to make three cauteries around the abdomen, as we have said in the bladder cautery and one cautery outside the back.
et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	 and let the cauteries be attached, as we have said.
de la hainche	Of the hernia
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble;	 When the moist thickeners descend into the haunch of the thigh, and for this reason it moves from its place, the signs are that the thigh is longer than the other when measured together.
et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle;	 And the joints to be treated should be found in the affected limb, so you must apply the fire cautery on the patient over the swelling area, similar to a circle, and position yourself before the joint around the swelling, as it turns, so that the swelling is inside the circle;
et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	 And the cautery should be similar to those used for stomach cauterization.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs;	 And if this type of cautery is not present, make three olive-sized large cauteries and ensure they are as sharp as all the others;
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Cure it until it becomes healthy.
de la dolor de la hainche	of the pain of the hernia
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene:	 When pain occurs in the swelling area, and it is due to cold and moisture, the patient is cured of this as we have said in the division, but the illness remains;
adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	 Therefore, it is necessary to purge the patient of large humors with foul-smelling pills, or other good-looking pills.
Aprés li fai cautere;	 After performing the fire cautery:
et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres:	 And the method of the cautery is according to two methods:
c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	 (This means) It is to be known together with burning medicines and the fire cautery.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz:	 Fire cautery is according to many methods, of which one is such:
que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire;	 You shall cauterize on the boil of the buttock with three triangular cauteries according to this shape, and make good depth and large, and have space between each cautery the thickness of a thumb, and let the cauteries be olive-shaped.
aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	 Sometimes they make a cauterization in the middle on the buttock's head, so there are four according to this shape.
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche;	 And if you see, if you cauterize with the circular cautery that we have mentioned before in the dislocation of the buttock.
mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	 But do it in this manner so that the circles encompass the entire buttock, and all its edges are burned.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	 And this is the manner in which it is done for sciatica, when the pain remains in the lower back, and does not reach as far as the thigh or leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc;	 And if it comes up to the thigh and leg, make two cauteries there where the patient says that the pain is, and the fourth cautery above the ankle four fingers wide, on the left side a little.
et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur;	 And let the cautery be the cutting tool, and heat the thickness of the coal.
et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	 And if the patient feels that pain spreads to the chest or near there, cauterize it at the place where he feels pain with a lance three or four fingers deep, which is called "poins".
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus;	 And if necessary, make more.
et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	 And if it is known that the pain is below the knee towards the thigh, perform a cautery using the cutting or circular lance; and take great care in all your cauteries to not let the cauterize too deeply so as not to burn the nerves and large arteries, and to do no greater harm or contraction to the patient.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	 And I myself have seen many who have performed a fire cautery on the heel of the foot, and they let it become swollen completely, both the leg and the feet, and all the toes were pierced and corrupted.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	 After a belly solution where death occurred.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	 And if the pain is in two parts together, perform a fire cautery on one and the other, according to this method.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce;	 And the sage (wise man) said in the cautery of the hainche (possibly referring to a part or disease), here is the method, make the iron similar to a small nail of the finger, or slightly smaller, and it should be cross-shaped or made from one crosspiece to another of a distance equal to the size of a nut of the thumb;
et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait;	 and let the crosspieces be above each other, and also like nuts, and have the iron piece well made.
et c’est li forme:	 and this is the shape:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit;	 And let it be heated until it is all red and glowing hot, and then place it on the box of the sick hainche (part or disease), and turn it towards the healthy side.
et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors;	 And the cautery once applied, let it heal for three days.
et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens;	 Then apply a poultice of butter, and keep the wound open for a long time.
aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	 After the treatment with ointment until it is healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent;	 Al-Bukassim says that we should not use this caution too much due to fear of its gaze, and few people use it.
et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	 And yet, this is a good cautery, which can be endured by the strong, and there where it adheres.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi;	 The medical cautery is such that you make the instrument between the joints in this way, by cutting through the margin of the door, and it should be of iron or steel with a long handle, and at the top have two notches, and between each one the width of the size of a thumb.
et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	 And they shall be open and above, and join together as shown in this form:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche;	 Place the bed of the backbone on the patient lying on his side, and then your hand a little above the bed of the backbone;
aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	 After casting between the two circles of hot iron heated in the firepot, and leave it for an hour, and let the patient endure the heat and the burn from it.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu;	 For it penetrates bite-like, just like fire;
et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit;	 And when the biting has passed, put your hand with the instrument and gently lift the backbone from its socket, and leave it thus for three days, and apply butter so that the blackness of the burn is removed;
et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait;	 And let it rest for three days until purulence comes out of it.
et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	 and this would be the last help after the treatment of sores, as long as they are healed.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument;	 And if the pain has spread to the thigh or to the leg, make an instrument to bind it according to what you have done in the haunch properly.
et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	 And this is the method for hot bandages, and I have written or explained how to correct medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	 Take alkali and hot live coal, as much of one as of the other, grind them together and put in a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir;	 or if it has a small opening that the point of a lance can enter into.
et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main;	 and put one pot on top of the other well filled, and put alkaline and salt and soft bandages on top, until there are two fingers' distance above the powders when you have firmly pressed it with your hand.
et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	 And let it remain like that until it dries and contracts or breaks open, then take all of that pus, and throw it onto lime and alkaline as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres.	 And when it has become very sore and is treated with various medicinal work and other cauteries for the limbs.
Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	 For it works like fire, and when treated with other medicines from which the inflammation is cauterized well, such as wax, tallow, honey, almonds, lime with soap, all mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	 And Galen tells us of a cure in which a man was cured from pain in the back and sciatic vein, and he praised it much, and said that no other cure was made for it, and that he became healthy once when this cure was done, and he bathed himself as indicated below.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie;	 And say thus: you take green powdered litharge (lime) and crush it very finely with a little fat, and place it on the inflammation and on the thigh and leg where the pain is, and let it stay.
et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	 And let it [the patient] rest for 3 hours, and in this time the patient no longer feels the burn.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	 Then make him enter or bathe until his body is slightly warmed, and have him lie down, and the pain will go away entirely and he will be healed.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	 And know that no one should use such fire cautery as medicine unless it is after the evacuation of the body.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout;	 And Dioscorides says that when the sciatic vein is burned with goat's-beard, it helps much;
et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	 and the cautery should be done in this manner.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	 Take linen and anoint it with old oil, and put it on the furrow that is between the little toe of the foot and the one called the cubital fossa.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;	 Take dry goat's-beard, heat it until it becomes coals, and place it on wool, and let it remain until it is cool.
et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;	 And do this again and continue to do so until you think by your senses that it has reached the hymen and the pain is stopped.
et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	 And this method of cautery is called "goat's-beard cautery".
de la dolor dou dos	Of the pain in the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, either by falling or impact or excessive evacuation, or from similar causes of cold matter spreading, none of these resemble cauteries unless for that which comes from the infusion of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	 It is necessary afterwards that the patient be emptied of fetid pills or similar things, which are placed on the back, where the pain is felt, three lines marked with a cross, and in each line V cauteries, or more according to the power and quantity that the patient can endure.
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	 and be done the cautery according to the cautery which is called "points".
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	 and if you see, do III or IV cauteries or IV at the cautery with an average shape according to this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	 Many times this disease comes to small children, and the signs of its beginning are that they have narrow anus when they strain, and fear.
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	 and you find in the lower spine of the back and in us the appearance that comes above the other spines.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and you want to cure it, cauterize it with the cautery of this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	 The cautery causes each part of the spine to enlarge.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	 And if you wish, cauterize around the spine with the cautery pointing two or three lines, and let the tips be close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	 After curing the joint until it is healthy, according to what we have said, beware not to administer the cautery in a lump that might be within a nerve.
de la dolor des jointes	of the pain in the joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	 When pains in the joints are due to swellings that affect every member of the body, and when pain comes in feet, which are called "gout" properly, and when it is caused by coldness and medicines cannot cure it, then it is cured by cauteries in this way:
fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	 make the patient hold a hot iron around the joint of the foot, and let the cautery be olive-shaped according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	 And if it is necessary to prick the abdomen, then the entire cautery is applied like "the point".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	 And if the pains come up to the knees and other joints, and this happens many times, make one or two cauteries on each part of the knee, with an olive-shaped cautery for each.
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	 and if you need more, then do more, but don't hold your hand away from the heated iron more than necessary.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	 And if the pains descend to the genitals and back, administer the fire cautery as we have said in its chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	 And if the pains are at the hands, make points around the wrist two lines.
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	 If there remains a point of pain in the fingers, make points above each joint and above the hair on the hand.
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	 And if the pains come as far as elbows or shoulders, cauterize each part and make good care of the patient and consider medications.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	 For if you take good care of him and purge pus, he will be saved with God's help.
de la routure dou syfac	From the rupture of the sifac
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	 When rot is coming in wounds and the boils descend to the joints and it is new, it is necessary that when you see it to cure, that he does not eat anything on that day.
et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;	 and that he uses things that relieve the stomach, so that the phlegm descends from his stomach.
aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;	 Afterwards make him sit on his back between your hands, and command him to hold his arm as long as the boils are healing, and you bind it with your fingers, and press down over the roture on the bone of the elbow, and at every sign that is similar to half a circle above the chest.
puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	 Then heat the fire cautery with this form:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	 until it is white and gives off a smell.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	 Then heat the iron rods at their place;
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	 and the assistant touches his hand so that he does not return backwards.
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	 and work well the thighs on the patient, put a cushion under him and a sergeant on his thighs, and another on the bed that supports his hands.
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	 then place the cautery on the spot with your whole hand, hold it straight and hold it until you reach the bone, and if you do not reach it the first time, try again until you reach the bone.
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	 be careful that the patient does not move when you perform the cautery.
que tu ne le brulasses;	 do not burn him;
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	 So that the patient does not die or suffer further harm.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	 And know that if you do not reach the bone with the cautery, your work is worth nothing.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	 And the fire cauteries for children should be fine-tuned according to their size, and the same goes for adults according to theirs.
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	 After three days of care, the leach from the fire cautery should be removed when the burn is healed.
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	 After treating with other medicaments until it is healthy, and the patient lies on his back for forty days so that the wound heals well.
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	 And it is necessary to let him rest for a long time so that the swellings do not protrude when he gets up to go into rooms.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	 And after forty days, when he wants to get up, they should prepare a bandage well and keep it for forty more days.
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	 And have good rest, let him work little and watch against excessive drinking and eating, and excessive shouting.
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	 And when he follows this teaching, he becomes entirely healthy.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	 And here I shall tell you about the treatment of amputation in its chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	of the wound from the belly
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	 When roundworms appear in other bellies and are known, and you see that they do not grow further, then perform the cautery of the cautery according to its quantity, and burn the third part of the liver.
aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;	 After the cure, as we have said.
et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	 And none of the ancients said it should be cauterized at the cautery with three corners according to this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	 However, mark first the location of the beginning and make a line above the boil, and another below it, and then place your hand on the entire cautery handle.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	 But the initial cauterizations are lighter and more mobile.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	of old pain in any member
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	 When pain comes in any limb, either from falling or being injured, and that pain lasts for a long time, and the medicines used do not help, it is necessary to cauterize with the cautery called "poins", and the cautery should be according to the length of the limb, its smallness and weakness, and its nature and location of twisting and of its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;	 if he is healthy from the first cautery, that's good.
se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	 If this name recurs for another cautery upon that one, because custom is that it should change in the limb that is near, therefore you must perform the cauteries as long as the patient remains ill.
de meselerie	To mix or compound (medicines)
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	 The illness is sometimes helped by cautery with great help, and the same applies to those who come from the rotting of phlegm and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:	 Can you see the patient to be cauterized, take care if the disease is at its beginning, and if it has been cured according to what we have said in the division, and neither it bleeds nor remains, and you doubt that the corruption will spread throughout the patient, then perform V cautery on the head.
I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous;	 I place one hand on the head and the other towards the forehead at the end of the hairs.
et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel;	 The first is placed on the temples, and the second behind the ears.
et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir;	 Keep your hand so that the cautery comes to the bone and so that the bark bursts out through it so that the vapors of the large humors can escape.
et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	 And cauterize the mice according to what is before [you].
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse;	 And if the fracture is scattered everywhere;
et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules;	 and it becomes manifest, then you must apply these cauterizations as we have said before, namely the cautery on the neck, the cautery on the spine of the neck, the six cauteries on the spine of the back, the large one on the shinbone and the other below it, and two cauteries on each shoulder;
et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains;	 And he shall stretch out the muscles, and he shall stretch out the tendons with the rod, and he shall stretch each joint of the hands and feet, and the hollows of the hands.
et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler;	 And protect the nerves that are above the last bone in the foot, that you not burn them;
et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	 Sometimes make an incision on the bone of the fist, and another one on the bone of the stomach, and another one on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite;	 And know that when you do more cauterizations, you do more good, and it benefits him more.
et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	 And know that the patient feels no pain during the cauterization as the body is already entirely corrupt.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	 And the cautery should be large and small according to the members and joints, as you will find in the manners of irons.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	 After curing the shoulder with flour and honey and other remedies until it is purified.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre;	 When swelling appears in any member and is treated with medicine, oil, and plasters, and it is not cured, then cauterize the member according to the size and smallness of the member.
et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur;	 And let the cautery be a small opening in the thick part of the flesh;
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	 then heal with ointments until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure;	 Sometimes they make a cautery at the hand, foot, and back, to the nerve that paralyzes the limb, and in this way the tumor is removed;
et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	 and no one should interfere unless they are knowledgeable about limbs and the paths of moving nerves in the body;
de albaras	Of swabs (or bandages)
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color;	 When the disease called "albaras" is evident, and the remedies of medicine are worth nothing, then cauterize with a deep cautery until the inflammation disappears, and the color becomes normal;
puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie;	 Then cook (or prepare) flour of wheat and lentils with rose oil and banana leaves, as well as the blood of a cat and the blood of a crane, each one in equal parts.
et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And let it be mixed together completely, tie it up in a cloth, and apply it to the place until it is healed.
li cure de chancre par cautere	They cure scrofula (scrofula is a term for a chronic skin disease, often associated with tuberculosis) through cautery.
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	 When a boil appears at the beginning, and you wish to stop it, if you cauterize with the cautery that resembles a circle around the boil.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre;	 However, the wise men also say that a fire cautery should be performed in the middle of the abscess.
et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois;	 However, this does not seem good to me, as I fear that it will become an ulcer and corrupt, and I have seen it happen once.
et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	 And the more appropriate thing is that it be cauterized around (the abscess), with the cautery called "circular", as we have said in the discussion about cauteries.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	The inflammation which cannot move
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens;	 When someone has a disease called "adubelati," and it delays healing or because of the excess it causes, or because of the age of the patient when they are decrepit (meaning very old), and there is little blood, or due to the time.
et tu la vues haster de meurer:	 and you see it hastened to heal:
adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant;	 then cauterize it around with many small cauteries by pricking.
aprés le laisse ensi.	 afterwards leave it in that state.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	 When it will hasten to heal. (Continuing from the previous translation)
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it pierced through entirely with the fire cautery, heat the cautery as follows:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	 And place your hand in the middle of this disease called "adubelati" while the cauteries have pierced through the core, and let the cauteries be such that the patient feels them outside to such an extent that the course of the pus is alleviated.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	 After curing completely when he is perfectly healthy.
li cure dou feu par fer	treatment with fire by iron
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	 Another kind of disease is called "corrosion," and it is nothing other than a rot of the member, because it consumes limbs as fire dries up dry wood.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est;	 If you see this disease in a place that can bear cautery with fire, then heat the cauteries slightly small and large according to what is required for the location or the disease.
aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	 afterwards cauterize it all over until you reach all the corruption and nothing remains of it, so that everything corrupt should be excised.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	 And then leave it for three days and put on the affected areas soft powder made with oil until burns from the fire are removed, and all the corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	 After the treatment of ointments causing heat.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin;	 And if after three days you see no pus healthy, it is good;
et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	 and if not, resume the cautery on that which remains in the corrupted joints.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu;	 And this lancet has sometimes been cured with medicinal juice instead of fire cautery.
mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division:	 nevertheless fire cautery is of greater aid, and I have already said the cure for medicinal juice in the division:
pren la quant tu en as mestier.	 take it when you need it.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	The hairs which come to the feet
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	 Often, through the foot, a disease called "clog" arises according to our understanding, which is a large thing that bites at the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	 And the cauteries for this disease are in two ways.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	 This is to know fire cautery, and hot water cautery.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;	 Fire cautery is heated like a feather from a ploughshare, and should be made of good iron to the extent that it can penetrate through all parts, and that its edges are thin.
aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou;	 Place it all hot on the nail, and turn your hand entirely around the nail until it reaches the base of the nail.
et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture;	 Leave it in this way for three days until it begins to emit pus.
puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	 Then make a poultice of wild herbs boiled with oil and leave it on all night; the nail will shrink and be uprooted from its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then heal the joint with a soothing ointment until it is healthy.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude;	 And if it is converted by foreign matter, and often happens in hands and feet, then you must apply hot cautery.
et est en teil maniere:	 It proceeds like this:
pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues;	 Take a cable of iron or wood, or a pin of lead, and place it on the nail and the anvil, that is, to pierce warts.
et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine;	 and place the cable above so that it goes all around, then put some hot paste there and hold your hand firmly, and press your hand while turning so that the edge of the cable comes to the root of the nail, and let the hot paste find its way deeply to the root.
et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre;	 make the patient endure the bite of the hot paste for an hour;
puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	 then leave it like that and it will fall out with all its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	 Similarly, do as you did before, until you scorch all those within the body; then heal the burns that cause pain.
li cure dou trembler	The cure for trembling
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee;	 If someone trembles due to cold or nerves, or from quarter fever or something else, you must do four fire cauterizations or four on the spine of the back, one between each spine.
et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire;	 And for the fire cautery, use it on the foot or on the stomach with an olive oil cauterization.
si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	 If he lets it tremble and hastens the healing of the cold disease.
des pustules puans	of putrid boils
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	 Sometimes, boils or putrid pustules appear on the body due to corrupt large matter.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule:	 It is necessary at first when they appear, that a cautery be made over each head of the pustule:
un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	 A subtle cautery made from myrtle staff, so that the point is seized by fire, or of the long root of Aristolochia, or with a cauterizing plier.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez;	 And sometimes they are cauterized at the beginning when they appear in this manner, and they cannot grow further, but the excess is torn off that comes from them, and they heal.
mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	 But it must be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	When the artery is cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses;	 Often there are great movements of blood from the artery which is cut at the wound that reaches the outside, or in the incision of an abscess, or to the cautery of a member, and similar things.
et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	 And it is a very bad thing to dislocate [something].
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus;	 Furthermore, when this happens to someone, quickly place your finger on the wound of the vein, and press it as hard as possible until the blood stops flowing.
puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge;	 Then apply the olive oil-filled fire cautery, both small and large, until they are all red.
puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	 Then take, whether large or small depending on the wound and the location in which the artery runs, and place the cautery on that vein where your finger is, and hold the cautery there until the blood clots.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement .i. autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if a jump occurs when you place your finger on the vein, and the cautery is extinguished, take quickly another one of the cauteries that are near the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez;	 And continue to do this one after the other until the blood stops flowing.
et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide;	 And beware not to burn the nerve that is exposed, and no other harm comes upon the patient.
et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit:	 And learn that when the artery is not cut through, it cannot be properly bandaged up if the artery is large, unless it's by one of the four ways we have mentioned.
ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;	 or by cautery, or by extraction when it is not treated, or by tightly tying thread, or by medicines applied that have the power to stop bleeding.
et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	 and bind and tighten accordingly.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Whoever applies tight bandages or places hot substances on it, or similar things, will not benefit if the above method does not help.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne;	 And if this happens and there is no mirror or medicine present, he should put his finger on the wound as we have said, and stretch it out accordingly until it stops bleeding over the wound and the vein.
et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez;	 And it should not move, but the cold dampness should often be cooled very much until the wound is frozen and swollen and hardened.
et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	 Make inquiries about what remedies and medications are needed for this case.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	Here begins the second book of surgical treatments.
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres;	 We have told you in the first chapter about all diseases where it is necessary to use a hot cautery or medication, and we examine the eyes, causes, instruments, forms of the cauteries.
et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	 And I have placed that chapter on the head to the feet, and I will go through this chapter in the same way because it is easier to find what we are looking for.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And as I begin this, it is necessary, dear child, that you learn that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the first of the cauterizations, and for this reason greater caution is required.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses;	 For in the work of this chapter, there is often the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and in cutting into stones, and similar things.
ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	 There is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	 And I warn you to not undertake foolishness.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	 For many ways of people come in the treatment.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice;	 Those who suffer such illnesses and die quickly due to the madness caused by their disease and the great severity of their condition.
et de ces doit on avoir paor.	 and one should fear such things.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit:	 And among these there are those who entrust their senses to you, and say:
«atendez, je sui garis»;	 "Attend, I am cured.
et li maladie est despitouse.	 and the illness is deceitful.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los;	 You should not easily trust those who come to you with this mannerism, but put more weight on your honor than your desire, and do not rashly believe but wisely from those about whom you are certain, and from which you can take and learn.
et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie;	 And make use of prognosis and indication in the treatment of your patients, so that health may be attained.
et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	 And this will help you to acquire good reputation, glory, and memory of praise.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Dearest son, may our Lords grant you good understanding and righteousness, and if you wish to aspire to the holy inspiration of His hand, amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	Moreover, I have organized this chapter in discussing by chapters, according to what is before the chapter of cauteries, which I have previously discussed from head to feet, because you will find it easier to understand those things that you may need.
dou chief plein d’aigue	The head full of water
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant;	 Note that this illness often comes upon children during birth, and when the head of the child is forced too tightly.
et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	 Sometimes it comes from causes that are not known.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors;	 I have never seen this illness outside of children, and the death hastens for all those that I have seen.
et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	 And because of this, it seems to me that I should be less active in these treatments.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir;	 And I saw an infant whose shoulder was full of water, and the head grew larger every day until it could no longer support.
et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os;	 And the moisture spread so much that he was dead, and this moisture is gathered under the bone above the syphilis, between the cartilage and the bone.
et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large;	 And the work is such that if there is moisture between the cartilage and the bone, and the abscess is small, you should make a wide incision near the head.
et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre;	 And let it be as long as ours, until the moisture runs out.
et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	 Look here is the shape of the probe (spatula):
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai .ij. fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is more swollen, and the abscesses are larger, make two incisions in the form of a cross, as follows:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut:	 If the moisture is under the bone and you see the signs that the head is opened on both sides, and it forms a sharp crack when you press with your hand from inside, then it has not healed.
si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	 It is necessary that you make three cuts in the middle of the head in this manner:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	 And after the incision, remove all moisture.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor;	 After binding the cuts with linen and powders, put vinegar and oil on them and leave them like that for five days;
puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	 Then unbind it and cure the wound with lancing and ointments, let the head swell up, and give the patient dry meat from a damp place to eat until the limb is comfortable and healthy.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue;	 And another way of incision is that you look where the abscess is large, and where the liquid collects;
car aucune fois est elle devant;	 for sometimes it is in front;
aucune fois derrier;	 sometimes it is behind;
aucune fois en destre;	 sometimes on the right side;
et aucune fois en senestre.	 And sometimes to the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir;	 Therefore, make an incision where the abscess is and empty the pus, and do as you can with it.
et warde que tu ne coper l’artere;	 And beware not to cover the artery.
et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	 And if there comes blood, let the patient die in a seemly manner through bleeding and evacuation of moisture.
de reume	of rheum
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les .ij. arteres.	When a disease called "catarrh" affects any of the eyes or at its worst, and the disease is old, and the medicine's cure does not help at all, then the last cure is the cautery with which two arteries will be touched.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief;	 Therefore, when you wish to cover [something], have the patient bend his head backwards.
aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel;	 After rubbing the area with a coarse cloth until the arteries appear, then tighten the patient's neck with the cloth.
puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues;	 Then look where the vein is biting, and the left and right sides are behind the ears, and the hands should be placed.
puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	 Then mark the joints with a cross, then strike both with a sharp spatula of two parts, until the cut reaches the bone, and this should be done at the wide part of the joint.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com .ij. dois au traver.	And if you see (it), push the spatula beneath the artery and strike it from above, cutting as deeply as two fingers' width.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	When the vein is cut, it jumps out without ceasing continuously upward.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os;	 And if the arteries do not open to the touch, then you must measure the space of three fingers, then mark and cut up to the bone.
et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere;	 And it is necessary to forcefully put out the blood which is 6 cubits, and by chance a little more or less, according to what the patient can bear, and the filling of the artery.
puis regarde la plaie:	 then observe the wound:
s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	 If it remains on the bone close to the skin and the abscess does not burst open, then hold and bind the wound and treat with ointment until it is healed.
de emigrainne	From migration
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When the old migraine comes with a sharp catarrh, due to moisture in the eyes and heat in the temples and ancient forsenee and similar things, and it is treated with medicines and cures, but none of them help, we should cut open the arteries of the temples and cauterize, as we have said.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit;	 And the method of extracting them is that the patient bends the hair on his temples, and listens to the artery that opens in the temple, for it opens well by its beating, and is easily found except in some men who are too cold.
et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement;	 and if it is found to be in place, the patient pulls his neck with some cloth, then rubs the area with rough fabric, and washes the area with hot water until the artery appears clearly.
puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	 then take the spatula as follows:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie;	 then gently scrape the skin until you see the artery, then pull it up towards the prongs and separate well the fabrics from both sides.
et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	 And if the arteries are thin, turn it to the point of the incisor, then strike that part according to the size of the two cheeks.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	 If it is not cut, it will not heal at all.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III;	 And drain blood from the six veins down to three.
et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc;	 And if the arteries are large, you must tie it with two strong silk threads, one at each side of the wound, for pus not to come before the stitching of the wound and bleeding stops.
puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez;	 Then strike the excess that is between the two ligatures in the same hour itself, and if you see fit, cauterize with a surgical knife as far as the bone until the shoulders are separated.
et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	 And this is the mature work, if the patient does not have a fever and is of a hot constitution.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors:	 The cautery (or burning tool) is aid for curing moisture:
por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	 it is of greater aid to those suffering from moisture.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites;	 For the extraction of arteries, one must fill the cavity with old cotton and put it firmly in place;
et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 and when they are loosened, you should treat them with dry medicines that cause heat, and with bandages until it is healed.
et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez;	 and if the artery is not sealed as you work on it, hurry to cover it with cautionery (or burning tool), or fill the cavity with vitriol (a chemical substance) and hold your hand over it so that the wound does not become infected.
et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient;	 and if you do not have that, place your finger over the wound until it freezes, then rub the wound with cold water until it stops, and hold it as necessary.
et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	 And the one who is moved and lighter in the extraction of the artery is that you cauterize the vein with this sharp cautery, but the incision should be well thickened to keep its heat for a longer time.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	For when the instrument is too thin, it retains less heat.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus;	 And between the two blades there should be a space of that size, and then when you have closed the two sides, and you hold the fire burning until it reaches the bone, and cut the vein in two places.
et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout;	 And they should be separated between the two shoulders, because it is not welded by this fire cautery altogether.
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	 and this is the shape of the cautery:
des larmes	Tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis;	 When the eyes of the hairs are flowing from the veins that are above the head of fire, and it does not benefit by medicine when one performs it, and you see the patient's face turn red, and you see his forehead shake like a shudder.
et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.	 and if they are tender and moist so that the hairs of paper are falling out, and the papery flesh is burnt, and scorched by the heat of tears, this treatment is required.
Et l’apelerent li ancien «cure contuse», et est que tu faices a rere au malaide qui a ceste maladie les poilz qu’il ait ou front, puis li fai III fendures ou front igalment selonc la longesce dou front;	 And they called it by the ancients "contused cure", and is that you make at the back of the patient who has this disease the hairs on his forehead, then you make three cuts evenly along the length of the forehead.
et soit l’une des fendures ausi com II doi tout emmi lou front en avalant aval jusc’a neif, et les autres II as II costelz par desus les papieres, et te garde de l’incision des arteres que sont as II costez par desus les papieres;	 And one of the fissures (should be) similar to the way it should move the entire forehead forward by swallowing downwards up to the nose, and the others will be in the chest through the papers above, and keep yourself from incising the arteries that are above the papers.
