et met sus les poudres une piece d’emplaustre de fort ou d’autre emplaustre soudant, et le laisse tant qu’il chiece par lui, puis le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	 and place a plaster piece of strong or other adhesive plaster on top of the powders, and leave it until it dries, then heal it with ointment until it heals completely.
Li maniere de la costure si est que tu assembles la solution:	 The manner of the stitching is that you assemble the suture:
ou par aguilles, si com nos avons dit en la costure dou ventre;	 or with needles, as we have said in the abdominal suturing;
ou par fil, si com je le t’ai fait savoir.	 or with thread, as I told you.
des apostemes des levres	of the lips of an abscess
A mains homes avient dedens les levres aposteme dur, semblans a grains de veces, et menor et plus grant;	 In men, an abscess hard inside the lips, resembling grains of wheat, both smaller and larger;
adonques couvient que tu tornes les levres, et fendes sus chescun nout, et le prent as pinceures et le cope en chescune partie;	 then it is necessary that you turn the lips, and make an incision above each tooth, and take them with the forceps and crush them in each part;
puis emple lou leu aprés l’incision de vitriole broiet, tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	 Then apply the lead after the incision of crushed vitriol, until the wound is cauterized.
et puis lou leive d’aisil, et cure lou leu de choses seches tant qu’il soit sanez.	 and then let it heal, and treat the lead with dry things until it heals.
de la char des gencives	From the jawbone
Maintes fois naist sus les gencives char ajostee, que li ancien apelent «albulus»;	 Many times a boil arises on the gums, which the ancients called "albulus".
si covient que tu la sostienes as tenailles, et la cope a sa racine, et laisse corre la bowe ou le sanc;	 it is necessary that you hold it with tweezers, and cut off its root, and let the pus or blood flow.
puis met sor le leu vitriole broiet, ou autres poudres restraignans et desiccatives;	 then apply crushed vitriol or other powders restraining and drying to the wound.
et se celle char revient aprés l’incision, et maintes fois avient, si la cope la seconde fois, et la cauterize:	 if the boil comes back after incision, which often happens, cut it again, and then cauterize it.
si ne revient mie aprés le cautere;	 if it does not return after cauterization.
et ce sont les formes des estrumens por coper.	 And these are the shapes of the instruments for covering.
des sordens	The sores
Aucunes fois sont assemblees au chief des dens, dedens la bouche entre les gencives, escorces qui sont laides et aspres;	 Sometimes sharp points are assembled at the teeth's roots, within the mouth between the gums, rough and harsh skins.
et aucune fois sont li dent noir et citrin et vers, tant que li corruption vient a la gencive, et sont li dent puant;	 And sometimes the teeth are black and greenish and curved towards each other, until corruption reaches the gum, and they rot.
si covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, et ses chiés soit en ton saint, et reis les dens ou les escorces aperent, tant qu’il n’i demore rien;	 It is necessary that you make the patient sit between your hands, and his head in your lap, and carefully separate the teeth or the rough skins until nothing remains.
et ensi fai de la noiror et de la verdor, et de la jaunice et des autres taiches, tant qu’elles soient mondees;	 And do this with the blackness and greenish areas, and the yellow and other stains, until they are cleaned.
et s’on oste ceu que i est a la premiere rasion, c’est boin;	 If you remove those that are at the first reason, it is good;
se ceu non, si rencomence a rere le secont jor et lou tier, tant que tu aies tout reis;	 If not, start again on the second day or the third, until you have everything set.
et saiches que li dent ont mestier de diverses formes d’estrumens por reire, selonc ceu que li oevre lou demoustre, por ceu que li raseur dont on reit defuer les dens ont autres formes que cil dont on reit entre les dens;	 And know that the teeth have need of various types of instruments for drilling, according to what the work shows, because the scalpel used to file down the teeth has different shapes than those used between the teeth.
et cestes formes et autres soient avec toi appareillies.	 and these forms and others should be with you prepared.
Il covient quant tu cures lou dent de sa dolor que tu tardes dou traire tant com tu pues, car ce ne doit om mie faire;	 It is necessary when curing the tooth of its pain that you delay the drawing as much as possible, for it should not be done at all.
car c’est une substance mout haute jusc’a donc c’on n’ait point d’excusation dou raier.	 because it is a very high substance up until then that one does not have any excuse for filing.
Adonques quant li malaides est constrains dou traire, si covient que tu soies certains dou dent doillant.	 Then, when the patient is compelled to draw (something), it is necessary that you are certain of the tooth pulling.
Maintes fois desoit li dolor lou malaide, et cuide qu’elle soit ou dent saint, et fait traire le boin dent;	 Many times the patient feels pain and believes it to be a toothache and pulls out the healthy tooth.
et toutevoie ne se depart mie li dolor per ceu, tant que li malvais estrais, car nos l’avons ja veut faire a ces sainors;	 And yet the pain does not part from him while the disease lasts, for we have seen it done with these noblemen.
et quant tu es bien certains dou dent doillant, si covient que tu escorches entor lou dent a tout i. spatumile fort por warder la gencive de toutes pars;	 And when you are certain about the tooth loosening, it is necessary that you scrape around the tooth all over.  Scraper strongly so as to protect the gums from all sides;
puis le mues a tes dois ou as tenailles subtilz au premier poc et poc, tant qu’il soit bien eslochiés, puis i afferme bien les tenailles;	 Then you move it with your fingers or subtle pliers at the very root and bit by bit, until it is well loosened, then you tighten the pliers well.
et soit li chiés dou malaide en ton saint entre tes genous, et lou tien bien si qu’il ne se mueve.	 And let the head of the patient be in your lap, and hold it so that it does not move.
Aprés estrai lou dent droitement sens brisier, et s’il ne saut fuer, si prent aucun de ces estrumens et le boute dedens de chescune part legierement, et lou remuef si com tu as fait premier.	 After straightening the tooth without breaking it, if it does not come out on its own, take any of these instruments and gently push it from each side, and move it as you have done before.
Et se li dens est perciez et mengiez, si covient que tu l’emplisses de drapelz, lai ou li pertus sont;	 If the tooth is pierced and eaten, then you must fill it with cloth where the holes are;
et si l’estraint subtilment as tenailles, que il ne brise a l’estraindre;	 And if you hold it gently with pliers so that it does not break while pulling.
et covient mout saigement ovrer entor la gencive por deschaucier lou dent.	 and it is necessary to apply great care around the gum to extract the tooth.
Et te done bien en warde que tu ne le brises, et en remaigne une partie, et reveigne au malaide par la malice de la racine plus grans dolors de la premiere.	 And be careful not to break it and leave a part of it, and the tooth will remain in place longer due to the mischief of the root, causing the patient greater pain than before.
Et te warde que tu ne faices mie ensi com font li ignorant sainor, qui par lor haste et par lor hardiesce brisent aucune fois le charreit, et n’i amenistrent mie ceu que nos avons conteit;	 And beware that you do not act as the ignorant do, who by their haste and recklessness sometimes break the cart, and do not bring what we have mentioned.
mais font venir aucune fois par l’oquison de ceu grant maladie por les racines que i demorent, ou por lou charreit qu’il brisent, si com nos avons sovent veut;	 but they sometimes bring about great illness through the use of these roots that remain in them, or by breaking the cart as we have often seen.
et quant li dens est trais, si lavez lou leu de vin ou d’aisil et de seil;	 and when the tooth is extracted, clean the area with wine or oil and linen cloth.
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, que sovent avient, si emple lou leu de vitriole broiet;	 if bleeding occurs afterwards, which often happens, use the area with ground glass.
et se ceu ne vaut, si le cauterize.	 And if it does not work, cauterize it.
Les formes des estrumens, a coi om muet les dens premier, soient a longes pointes et a gros mainches, qu’il ne doublent mie quant tu trairas le dent;	 The shapes of the instruments, with which you silence the teeth first, should be long points and large handles, lest they double when you extract the tooth.
et ce sont les formes:	 and these are their forms:
Et soient de gros membres si qu’il ne ploient mie au traire, et soient de fer inde bien fait, et soient dentez por mues tenir.	And be large enough so that they do not bend when pulling, and be made of good iron, and be toothed for gripping.
de la racine des dens	of the root of the teeth
Quant li racine demoure au traire, si covient que tu mettes sor le leu coton moilliet em burre I jor ou II, tant que li leus soit amolis, pues i boute les tenailles qui sont apelees «algefri», de coi li chiés semblet bec de soigne;	 When the root remains when extracting, it is necessary that you put on top of it damp cotton in butter for a day or two, until the tooth loosens, then insert the pliers called "algefri", with which the teeth seem to be like tweezers.
et soient dedens faites ausi com une lime et c’est li forme:	 and within them should be made like a crowbar and this is their form:
Et se les racines ne vuellent issir a tout ces tenailles, si covient que tu descuevre la char tot entor la racine, et i met l’estrument qui est apelez «althali», c’est a savoir palainche, de coi ci est li forme:	And if the roots do not want to come out with all these tools, then you must expose the flesh all around the root, and place the instrument called "althali," which is known as forceps, in this shape:
Et soit fors et gros si qu’il ne brise mie, et se li racine saut par ceu, c’est boin;	 And it should be out and large so that it does not break, and if the root jumps through them, it is good.
se ceu non, si t’aide de toz les estrumens, de coi les formes vienent ci aprés:	 If not, help with all instruments, so that the forms come afterwards:
Et si s’aide on de cest estrument qui ait .ij. rains, de coi ci est li forme:	And if you aid with this instrument having two arms, in this shape:
et d’autres ferremens qui sont devant en la rasion des dens, et de cest estrument qui semble unes grans tenailles, dont ci est li forme:	And other instruments which are before the teeth, and of this tool that appears like large pincers, whose shape is as follows:
Et soit cist estrumens fors qu’il ne puisse brisier, et saiches que mout d’estrumens de dens sont;	 And let this instrument be other than one that can break, and know that many dense instruments are.
et ausi d’autres estrumens, qui ne sont mie contez;	 and also with other instruments, which are not counted;
et li saiges maistres subtilz trueve par soi meisme son estrument, selonc ceu que ses ovraiges et li maladie li demoustre, car il i a de teilz maladies ou li ancien n’enseignerent point d’estrument por la diversiteit d’au;s et s’om brise point dou charreit ou des autres os, ou il porrit, si i cerche as estrumens qu’il i covient, que je t’ai dit, et t’aide des gestes, de coi ci est li forme:	 and the wise masters discover by themselves their instrument, according to what their work and the illness show, for there are such diseases where the ancients did not teach any instrument due to diversity of ailments, and if it breaks the cart or other bones where it should not, it searches among the instruments that it needs, which I told you, and helps with gestures, so here is the form:
Et soient gros et bien tenant por tenir l’os, qu’il n’eschaipe, mais le puisse tenir et oster;	 And let them be large and firm to hold the bone, so that it does not slip away, but can be held and removed.
et puis restoure lou leu de medicines convenant a ceu, et s’il ait en l’os porriture, et elle est petite, si la reis a tout cest estrument:	 And then restore the joint with suitable medicines, and if there is pus in the bone, and it is small, press all this instrument:
Quant li dent apperent ne mie selonc lou cors natureil, et li forme est laide, et meismement en femmes puceles, si covient que tu saiches se li dens est neis aprés lou dent, et n’est mie en droit leu, et on ne lou puet soier ne limer:	 When the teeth appear not according to natural form, and the shape is ugly, especially in young women, it is necessary that you know if the teeth are not born after the gum, and are not in the correct place, and cannot be corrected or filed:
adonques lou raie;	 Therefore extract the tooth.
et s’il est aers avec lou dent, si prent cest estrument dont ci est li forme, et est semblans a I petit bec, et soit de fer inde agut en som:	 If it is near the gum with the tooth, take this instrument shaped like a small beak, and made of sharp iron at the end:
Et lou cope poc et poc em mains jors por la duresce dou dent, et por ceu que tu ne mueves les autres, et s’il est apparans c’on le puisse limer, si lou lime d’une teil lime com ci est li forme:	And the handle of the chisel should be held often for the hardness of the tooth, and because you do not move the others, and if it appears that one can file it, file it with a small flat file as shown here:
et est ausi com li lime de coi on fait les aguilles;	 And it is as if the limb of which one makes needles.
et en lime lou dent poc et poc em mains jors legierement, si qu’il ne se mueve tant qu’il chiece;	 And in grinding the tooth, press and press lightly by hand, so that it does not move while chewing.
puis la plaine en la fin a tout aucun raseur, et se li dens est trop trenchans et il blece la lengue, si covient limer l’aspreteit tant qu’il soit igalz, si qu’il ne blece la lengue ne ne corrompe la parole.	 Then, flatten the end with any file, and if the tooth is too sharp and it bites the tongue, it must be ground smooth until it is even, so that it does not bite the tongue or corrupt speech.
quant li dent lochent	When the teeth are loose
Quant li dent devant lochent, ou par percussion ou par cheoir, et li malaides ne puet presser sus ceu qu’il menjue qu’il ne chient, et tu les as curez de medicines restrignans, et ceu ne vaut;	 When the teeth loosen in front, either from percussion or falling out, and the patient cannot press down on it while eating so that it does not fall out, and you treat them with constricting medicines; this is of no use.
si les covient restraindre d’un fil d’or, car li filz d’argent devient vert et porrit, mais li ors ne se mue onques;	 If it must be held in place with a golden thread, for silver threads become green and rot, but gold never does.
et soit li filz moiens ne trop gros ne trop menus, selonc la quantiteit de l’espaice entre les dens;	 And let the son be neither too thick nor too thin, according to the size of the space between the teeth.
et se tu vues adrecier les dens, si pren lou fil et lou boute double entre les II dens sains, puis met les chiés entre les dens meus, s’il en i a I ou plusors, tant que tu veignes saigement jusc’au dent sain d’autre part;	 And if you wish to align the teeth, take the thread and double it between two healthy teeth, then place the chisels between the lower teeth (if there are one or more), as far as you can see clearly until the healthy tooth on the other side.
puis rencomence la coverture jusc’a la partie ou tu encomensas, et estrains ta main subtilment et saigement, tant qu’il ne se mueve point;	 Then continue covering up to the part where you began, and press your hand gently but firmly, so it does not move.
et soit ta lieeure a la racine dou dent si qu’il ne puist eschaper.	 And tie the ligature to the root of the tooth so that it cannot escape.
Puis cope les chiés dou fil a unes tenailles, et les assemble, et les repont entre le dent sain, et le met ensi qu’il ne blece la lengue;	 Then cut the chisels with the thread using the pliers and assemble them, then place them between the healthy tooth and the dislocated tooth so that it does not bite the tongue.
et puis le laisse ensi estroit tant com il puet demorer, et s’il deslie, ou li filz ront, si l’estraint d’un autre fil;	 And then let it remain as tight as it can endure, and if it slips or comes undone, tie it again with another thread.
si demorrait et servira ensi tout son tens, et c’est li forme des dens et li figure de l’adrecement des II dens sains, et des II meus, si com tu vois:	 If it remains and serves in this way for its entire duration, it is the shape of teeth and the alignment of the two healthy teeth or the two molars, as you can see.
Et quant li dent chiet, si lou remet on en son leu, de fres en fres, si com nos avons dit;	 And when a tooth falls out, put it back in its place, freshly, as we have said.
et ne s’en entremette mie qui n’est saiges et soffrans, et aucune fois fait on la forme d’un dent d’os de vaiche, et lou met on au leu ou li defaute est, et l’estraint on si com nos avons dit, et demore et sert ensi lonc tens.	 And do not meddle with it unless one is wise and experienced; and never make the shape of a tooth from animal bone, and put it in the place where it is lacking, and tie it as we have said, and remain and serve for a long time.
de coper lou liien de la lengue	Cover the ligament of the tongue
Aucune fois est cist liiens qui vient desoz la lengue ou naturez, que on naist ensi;	 Sometimes this link comes from under the tongue or naturally;
ou par accident de plaie soudee;	 or through an accidental wound healed;
et li ovraiges est telz que tu oevre la bouche dou malaide, et ait sa teste en ton sain, et li lieve la lengue;	 and the operations are such that you open the mouth of the patient, hold his head steady, and pull out the tongue;
puis cope lou liien nervous dou large, tant que li lengue soit desloie de son tenement, et se il i a duresce ou nout, et c’est de soudement de plaie, si i boute l’uncine et cope dou large celui liement;	 then grasp the nervous link firmly, as long as the tongue is dislocated from its place, and if there is hardness or swelling, and it is due to a sudden wound, insert the forceps and grasp the dislocated part firmly;
et garde que li fendure ne soit mie trop em parfont, por l’artere qui est desoz;	 and be careful that the incision is not too deep, because of the artery that is below;
et quant tu as fait, si leve le leu d’aigue rose et d’aisil, ou d’aigue froide, puis met desoz la lengue une tente de lin;	 and when you have done this, raise the head of a warm and soft poultice or a cold one, then put a linen cloth under the tongue;
et la teigne li malaides chescune nuit, que li leus ne puisse soder.	 And the itch afflicts the patient every night so that the joint cannot heal.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si met sor le leu vitriole broiet;	 If a discharge of blood comes, apply powdered vitriol to the joint.
et se li sans te vaint, si le cauterize au cautere lentiginout, qui est boin a ceu;	 And if there is no discharge, cauterize it with slow-burning cautery, which is good for this purpose.
puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez,	 then heal it with other treatment until it heals.
et se tu lou vois de fusse color ou noir ou dur, si que li malaides ne lou sent, si n’i touchier point, car c’est chancre;	 If you see it swell with a dark or hard color, and the patient does not feel it, do not touch it because it is cancerous.
et s’il est declinans a blenchor, et il i a moistor, si i giete l’oncine, et lou fent d’un spatumile subtil, et lou delivre d’une part et d’autre;	 If it is bending towards swelling and there is moisture, pour on oil, and cut it open with a sharp instrument from both sides.
et se li sans te vaint a ton ovraige, si met sus vitriole broiet tant qu’il soit estainchiez, puis revien a ton ovraige tant que tu traies tout fuer;	 And if the bone dares to oppose your work, lay vitriol powder on it until it is cauterized, then return to your work as soon as you draw all the fire.
puis leve lou leu d’aisil et de seil, et le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then lift up the limb and heal it with other treatments until it is healed.
des apostemes de la gorge	abscesses of the throat
Aucune fois vient dedens la gorge boces qui sont apelees «godath», et les apele on proprement les II amandres, et quant tu les cures, si com nos avons dit en la division, et elles ne sont sanees, si pren garde:	 Sometimes boils called "gogath" appear in the throat, and they are properly called the two almonds. When you cure them, as we have said in the division, and they do not heal, be careful.
se c’est apostemes dur de petit sens et de fusse color, si ne lou touchier mie de fer.	 If it is a hard abscess of small size and dark color, do not touch it with iron.
Et s’il est rouges et li racine est grosse, si ne lou touchier mie de fer, ausi por lou decorrement de sanc;	 And if it is red and the root is large, do not touch it with iron, also for the flow of blood.
mais lou laisse tant qu’il soit meur, et adonques tu lou partiras, ou il rompirait par soi;	 But let it remain until it is dead, and then you will cut it off, or it would break by itself.
et s’il est de blainche color reont, et li racine est subtilz, si aies apareilliet l’estrument por coper, mais regarde premierement se li apostemes chalz repose et est apaisiez.	 And if it is of white color and the root is subtle, you should prepare the instrument for covering, but first check whether the abscess has cooled down and been pacified.
Adonques fai seoir lou malaide devant lou soleil, et ses chiés soit en ton sain, et li oevre la bouche et lou preigne li serjans entre ses mains, et presse la lengue desoz a tout l’estrument, de coi ci est li forme;	 Then have the patient sit before the sun and his shoulder in your hand, open his mouth, and the servant takes it between his hands, pressing the tongue beneath the entire instrument, which is its shape.
et soit d’argent ou d’arain subtil ausi com uns coutelz:	 And it should be made of silver or fine bronze like a knife:
Cant tu presses la lengue a tout cest estrument, et tu vois l’aposteme, si pren l’oncine et lou fiche en l’amandre, et la trai fuer au desus plus que tu pues;	 Can you press the tongue against the entire instrument and if you see an abscess, take the hook and insert it into the wound, pulling it out towards the top more than you can.
et trai aucune chose des toiles avec, puis la cope a l’estrument, de coi ci est li forme, que semble unes forces;	 And pull no thing with threads from it, then seize it at the instrument, thus is its shape, which seems like a handle;
et toutevoie li chief sont corbé, et l’un endroit l’autre, et sont molt agut, et est fait de fer inde ou d’andainne:	 And the head bends and twists in one direction to another, and they are very sharp, and it is made of iron or bone;
Et se tu n’as cest estrument present, si lou cope as tenailles, de coi ci est li forme:	And if you do not have this tool present, use pliers of this shape:
Et soit trenchans d’une part, et d’autre part nom;	 And be called cutting from one side, and from the other called notching;
et quant tu as copeit l’une des amandres, si cope l’autre selonc cele meisme maniere, et aprés l’incision gargarize li malaides aigue chaude, et aigue et aisil, et se decorremens de sanc avient, si gargarize li malaides aigue, ou escorces de pomes grenates soient cuites, ou fuelles de mirte, et semblans choses, tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	 And when you have seized one of the almonds, seize the other in the same way, and after the incision, pour hot sharp and acid liquid on the patient's wound, which causes bleeding, pour hot acid or pomegranate rind cooked or myrtle bunches, or similar things, until the blood is stopped;
puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	 Then let the cure until it heals;
et aucune fois naissent en la gorge autres apostemes que les II amandres, si les cope donques ensi com les II amandres igament.	 And sometimes in the throat other abscesses than two mandibles grow, so prick them accordingly like two mandibles equally.
Et je medicinai une femme d’un aposteme que li estoit neis dedens la gorge, c’est a savoir I aposteme de petit sens;	 And I treat a woman with an abscess that was born within the throat, namely an abscess of small size.
et avoit jai bien pres close toute la gorge, si que li femme ne pooit expirer por le conduit qui estoit estoupez, et ne pooit ne mengier ne boivre, et fust morte s’elle demorast ensi I jor ou II.	 and had the throat closed entirely, so that the woman could not exhale through the narrowed passage, nor eat or drink, and would have died if she stayed in such condition for a day or two.
Et li apostemes estoit jai si montez qu’il avoit fuer mis II rains par les II pertuis dou neis.	 And the abscess was so swollen that it had risen to two fingers above the two openings of the throat.
Je hastai donques tantost, et fichai en l’un I oncine, puis lou traï fuers, et en traï grant porcion de bowe;	 So I had to hasten and prick one onyx, then pull it out, and pull a large piece of pus from it.
puis refis autreteil en l’autre pertus dou neis, et li ovrai la bouche et li pressai la lengue;	 Then reset the other part in the opposite dislocation, and force open the mouth and squeeze the tongue;
aprés fichai l’oncine en ces apostemes, et en copai une partie, et n’en issit fuers que un poc de sanc;	 Then insert a needle into these abscesses, take some pus, and do not let any blood come out except a little;
et ensi fut destoupez li conduis de la gorge la femme, et comensa maintenant a boivre aigue et puis vin, et ne cessai de taillier de cel aposteme par lonc tens;	 and thus the throat of the woman was pierced, and she began to drink water and then wine, and did not stop cutting this abscess for a long time;
et li apostemes recroissoit adés, et remplissoit lou leu que je avoie vuidiet, tant qu’il refut mout gros;	 The abscess recurred again and filled the space I had intended, until it became very large;
adonques je l’engignai et lou cauterizai dedens la gorge:	 Then I tricked him and burned him inside his throat;
ensi demora sens croistre;	 Thus it remained swollen for a long time.
et me partis de ces parties, et ne soi que Deus fist de li aprés moi.	 And I left those parts and let God do with them as He willed after me.
de l’uve	Of the eye
Quant reume dessent a l’uve, et elle est enflee et elle est longe, si est apelee «perpendiculaire»;	 When the rectum protrudes to the anus, and it is swollen and long, it is called "perpendicular".
et s’elle est desoz grosse et reonde, si est apelee «uve».	 And if it is below large and round, it is called "bladder".
Quant elle est curee si com nos avons dit en la division, et li cure ne profite mie, et tu vois que li chaus apostemes est apaisiez, et elle est subtilz, si covient que tu la copes;	 When it is cured as we said in the previous section and the treatment does not benefit, and you see that the swellings abscesses have subsided, and it becomes subtle, then you should cut it.
et celle qui est reonde assemblee et n’est mie longe;	 And if it is round but not long, it assembles together.
et elle est sanguine ou de fusse color ou noire, si covient que tu eschues l’incision de li.	 If it is red or of mixed color or black, then you must make the incision.
Car il i a grant peril sus lou malaide.	 For there is great danger for the patient.
Il covient donques, quant tu la vois, selonc la maniere que j’ai dit, de sa blenchor et de sa longesce, que tu faices seoir le malaide devant lou soleil, et li presse la lengue a l’estrument dont nos avons fait la remembrance ci devant;	 Therefore, when you see it as I have said, in terms of its color and length, you should make the patient sit before the sun and press the tongue to the instrument that we mentioned before.
puis fiche l’oncine en l’uve, et la trai desoz, et la cope a I des II estrumens que j’ai dit en l’incision des II amandres.	 Then pierce the eye of the onion into the eye, and draw it out, and press it at the bottom in the incisions of the two almonds that I have said.
Et covient que tu ne coper mie fuer que la superfluiteit qui est outre le termine natureil;	 And it is necessary that you not cover any superfluity that is beyond the natural limit;
car se tu en copes plus, si grieves a la voix, et a la parolle;	 for if you cover more of it, it hurts the voice and speech;
et aprés l’incision, use de ceu que nos avons dit en l’incision des II amandres, et le cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	 After the incision, use what has been said in the incisions of the two almonds, and treat it until it is healed.
Et se li malaides a paor dou coper, si covient que tu i use d’engien a la cauterization de li sens paor.	 If the patient fears covering (it), then you must use an engine for the cauterization to allay his fear.
Et li maniere dou cautere si est aigue ague.	 And the method of cauterizing is with hot iron.
Et est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, et puis li presse la lengue a l’estrument que nos avons dit ou chapistre de cautere, et confis avec aigue vive chaus, si qu’elle ne soit mie trop espesse ne trop clere;	 And it is that the patient places their head in your lap and then you press the tongue with the instrument that has been said in the chapter of the fire cautery, and cauterize with live hot iron, but not too thick nor too thin.
et en emple le chevement de cest estrument, de coi ci est li forme:	 And use the application of this tool, which is shown here in its form:
Et ait ou chief une cheveure ou om met la medecine, si com li chevemens d’une cuillier, et met l’estrument a tout la medicine sus l’uve;	 And place a hair or a spoon with the medicine, as the handle of a spoon, and put the tool all over the medicine on the ulcer.
et li malaides soit gisans sus son costeit, si que li salive et li muscillaige corre de sa bouche de la medicine dedens, si qu’ele ne dessende a la gorge, et lou blece;	 The patient should lie on his side so that the saliva and mucus flow from his mouth into the medicine without it reaching the throat or the bladder.
puis tien ta main a tout la medicine et la presse sus l’uve, la quantiteit de la moitiet d’une houre, tant que tu la vois nercie et li mordications de la medicine soit apaisie;	 Then hold your hand over the whole medicine and press it on the ulcer for the amount of half an hour until you see it scab over and the pain from the medicine is alleviated.
et se tu vues, pren coton et l’envoloupe sus aucun estrument, et moille lou coton en la medicine, et boute l’estrument a tout le couton en la cainne desus, tant que li coton s’aerde sus l’uve;	 If you see the scab, take cotton and wrap it around some instrument, moisten the cotton in the medicine, and push the instrument all over the cotton onto the ulcer until the cotton adheres to the ulcer.
et fai ceu sovent, tant que li cauteres soit parfais, puis la laisse elle seche, et chiet aprés IIII jors ou V.	 And often do this while the cautery is still hot, then let it dry, and lie down afterwards for 4 or 5 days.
Et se tu as mestier de rencomencier lou cautere de la medicine, si le rencomence, et aprés le cautere l’essue entor l’uve, de couton embut em burre, et mundifie ceu qui est entor de la medicine;	 If you need to start the cautery of the treatment again, do so, and after the cautery, let the blood flow around the eye, with a linen cloth in butter, and clean what is around the treatment.
et soit arosez d’aigue froide, et soit curez de gargarismes tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And wash with cold water, and be cured by gargling until it heals.
Ceste cure est plus save de l’incision, ne que li cautere;	 This cure is more effective than incision, rather than cautery.
s’elle est curee de fumigation selonc ceste maniere, pren calament et ysope et origanum et rue et camomille et avronne et semblans herbes, et les assemble toutes ou aucunes d’eles en I pot, et i met aisil, et fai bullir;	 If it is cured by fumigation in this way, take calamint, yarrow, origanum, rue, chamomile, wormwood and similar herbs, and put them all together or some of these in one pot, add ashes, and boil.
et li potz soit bien gluez de fort terre, et enmi le pot ait I estrument cheveit selonc ceste maniere:	 And let the head be tightly packed with strong earth, and within it place an instrument of hair according to this manner:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain, et soit li uns des chiés boutez en la bouche dou malaide tant que li vapor monte a l’uve par la caine, tant que li uve soit mortifie;	 And let it be of silver or lead, and one of the shoulders pressed into the mouth of the patient until the steam rises to the eye through the channel until the eye is destroyed.
aprés lou rencomence sovent, tant que li uve seche, et garde que tu ne faices ceu au comencement de l’avenement de l’aposteme chaut, car plusors choses i avienent;	 After the start, often when the egg dries out, and be careful not to do it at the beginning of the abscess's eruption (breakout), as many things happen.
et ne faire mie ceu fuer que a la declination d’aposteme chaut.	 and not do it before the decline of the abscess breakout.
Et se cist estrument n’est presens, si pren une caine et met dedens lou chief une craiffe d’uef, si que li bouche au malaide n’ait mie trop chaut;	 And if this is not present, take a rope and put inside the head of an egg yolk so that the mouth of the patient does not become too hot.
car li craiffe d’uef ne lait mie la vapor grever la bouche, et c’est bone cure ensamble salut.	 as the egg yolk cradle does not let the vapor burden the mouth, and it is a good cure together with safety.
Maintes fois s’aert a la gorge os ou espinee de poisson, ou aucune chose;	 Many times it turns into the throat bone or fish spine, or something else;
si covient donc que tu traies ceu que tu pues veoir, et li presse la lengue au soleil a tout l’estrument, si que tu voies mues la chose;	 Therefore, you must pull out what you can see, and press the tongue against the sun with all the instruments until you see the thing move.
et ceu que ne t’apert mie et est reponus en la gorge, covient que tu faices vomir le malaide ainsois que li viande soit cuite en l’estomac;	 And if it does not open by itself and is replaced in the throat, you must make the patient vomit as soon as the food is cooked in the stomach.
par aventure si istra li chose aerse par le vomissement;	 In case of emergency, use vomiting to resolve this issue.
ou li malaides englutisse une piece d’esponge, ou une piece de navel, ou une racine de laitue, ou I morceil de pain sec;	 or if the patient swallows a piece of sponge, a piece of cork, a lettuce root, or a piece of dry bread.
et lie a l’esponge I fil, et puis la transglutisse;	 and tie it with thread, and then swallow it.
et quant elle venra au leu, si s’aerdra, et puis trairas fuer;	 when it reaches the place, it will swell, and you will draw it out.
et s’elle ne vient fuer de ceu que nos avons dit, si pren I estrument de plonc selonc ceste forme:	 if it does not swell as we have said, take a plum-shaped instrument according to this form.
Et soit li estrumens corbés au chief si qu’il puist plus legierement entrer en la gorge, et ait le chief en haut leveit;	 And the instrument should be curved at the top so that it can enter more easily into the throat, and have the tip raised.
et warde que tu ne touchier l’epiglote, que li tous ne li viegne, ne ne bouter mie l’os dedens;	 And beware not to touch the epiglottis, lest all does not live, nor push the bone inside.
et mues vaut que li malaides i boute l’estrument, por ceu qu’il seit mues ou li chose est aerse;	 It is better that the patient pushes the instrument, because it should move or the thing will be broken.
si la boute aval, ou il la traie fuer a tout l’estrument igalment, tant qu’elle soit fuer.	 if he pushes downward, or pulls it forward equally, all along the instrument, until it is out.
de la sansue de la gorge	the vein of the throat
Aucune fois est medicinee li sansue, si com j’ai dit en la division, par la cure de medicines;	 Sometimes, bloodletting is the medicine, as I have said in the division, by the treatment of medicines;
et quant ceu ne profite mie, adonques regarde en la gorge dou malaide au soleil, puis que tu li presses la lengue a l’estrument que je t’ai dit.	 And when that does not help, then look in the throat of the patient towards the sun, and you will press the tongue with the instrument I told you about.
Et se tu vois la sansue, si la trai a tout I petit uncine, ou as tenailles subtilz que valent a ceu.	 And if you see the pus, pull it out very gently, or use subtle tweezers that are suitable for this purpose.
Et se ceu ne vaut, si pren une caine chevee, et la boute en la gorge dou malaide, puis boute ou chevement de la caine I fer chaut, et fai ce sovent.	 And if that does not work, take a hairy rope and put it in the throat of the sick person, then insert or push into the throat the hot iron several times.
Et se teigne li malaides d’aigue toute jor.	 And let the patient drink water all day long.
puis pren plein I voirre d’aigue froide, et oevre la bouche, et la giete ens sens englutir, et la mueve a sa main sovent;	 Then take full glass of cold water, open the mouth, and throw it in to swallow, and move it with your hand often.
et si tost com li sansue sent l’aigue, si chiet.	 And as soon as the wound feels wet, it falls (down).
Et s’elle ne chiet si com nos avons dit, si subfumige lou malaide d’asefetide, a l’estrument que j’ai dit en la fumigation de l’uve;	 If it does not fall down as we have said, then you should afflict the patient with an afetoide of the eye using the instrument that I mentioned in the fumigation of the eye.
fai ceu maintes fois, car elle cherra sens targier.	 Repeat this often, for it needs to be carefully examined.
Et li maniere de la fumigation si est que tu preignes I pot ou il ait charbons vis, et soit li pos covert d’un coverseil perciet en mileu, et en celui pertus soit li chiés de l’estrument;	 The method of fumigation is that you take the pot which has burning charcoal in it, and cover it with a perforated cloth in the middle, and in that put the head of the instrument.
puis i giete ta fumigation, et li malaides mette lou chief de la cainne en sa bouche, et cloie la bouche, si que li fumee n’en isse mie, mais viegne jusc’a la sansue;	 Then pour out your fumigation, and the patient places the end of the pipe in his mouth, and closes his mouth so that the smoke does not escape but comes directly to the wound.
et la sansue cherra maintenant, et s’elle ne chiet, si rencomence la fumigation par maintes fois;	 And now the wound needs to be opened, and if it does not drain, then repeat the fumigation many times.
et soffre li malaides soif, et menjuce choses salees et als, et ne boive point d’aigue;	 The patient should endure thirst, eat salty things and almonds, and drink no water.
et adonques li iert mestier qu’elle isse fuer par cest governement.	 And then it will be necessary for it to issue forth according to this government.
Et li forme de l’estrument a coi on trait la sansue, si est, quant on la puet veoir, semblans a tenailles corbés por mues entrer en la gorge;	 The shape of the instrument used for draining pus is, when it can be seen, resembling curved tweezers to enter into the throat.
et ait semblance au bec de soigne, et i ait asperiteit de lime, si que ceu qu’elle prent, elle ne puet lassier;	 and have the form of a surgical needle, and be coated with lime, so that what it takes, it cannot release.
et vez ci la forme:	 observe this shape here:
li chapistres des apostemes	Chapter on abscesses
Mout de semblances d’aposteme sont, selonc ceu que li remembrance vient ci aprés d’un et d’autre en cest livre, et sont diver en perforation et en taille;	 The shape of abscesses is similar to those that memory brings after this in the book, and they differ in perforation and cutting.
et c’est en II manieres dont l’une est en sa semblance meisme, et de ceu qu’il tient moistor.	 And it is in two ways, of which one is similar in shape and from that which holds moisture.
Et li seconde maniere si est por les leus ou il sont au cors.	 And the second way is by the joints that are on the body.
car li apostemes dou chief est autres que cil dou fondement, et li apostemes dou leu charnut est autres que cil qui vient en jointures, et chescuns ait son jugement en l’uevre.	 For abscesses of the head are different from those on the base, and abscesses in the shoulder blade are different from those that come at the joints; each should have its judgment in the work.
Et si a apostemes c’on ne doit mie percier, tant que li bowe est meure selonc son acomplissement;	 And if an abscess should not be pierced, wait until the bubble is ripe according to its completion.
et si a de telz qu’il covient percier quant il sont crut, et ne meurent mie selonc lor acomplissement, si com aposteme qui sont delez jointures.	 and if there are those that should be pierced when they have matured, but do not die before maturity, such as abscesses which are dislocated from joints.
Car quant apostemes vient delez jointures, et on le laisse tant qu’il est porris entor, par aventure si sont corrumput li liien et li nerf de la jointure, par coi ce est cause de contraction en celui membre.	 For when an abscess appears at the joints and is left until it bursts, inadvertently the ligament and nerve of the joint may be corrupted, which causes contraction in that member.
Ou li aposteme est delez lou membre principel, et se tu tardes la perforation tant qu’il soit meurez, si nuira au membre principeil;	 For if the abscess is detached from the main member and you delay the piercing until it has matured, the main member will suffer.
ou il est delez lou fondement, si le perce on ainsois qu’il soit meurs;	 or if it is detached from the foundation, pierce it before it becomes mature.
et ne covient mie que tu perces aposteme crut sens digestion acomplie, fuers que celui qui est delez lou fondement, qu’il ne porrisse em parfont, et soit alongiez dedens, et i viegne fistule;	 It is not good to pierce a mature abscess without complete digestion, except for one that is detached from the foundation which cannot be closed and has an internal fistula.
et ne puisse saner en grant termine.	 And cannot heal completely.
Et covient que tu saiches l’oure de la perforation de l’aposteme qui est meur selonc l’acomplissement, et c’est quant li dolor est apaisie, et li departemens de la fievre, et l’amenuisement de la dolor et de la roujor, et dou debatement et de l’aguisement dou chief de l’aposteme, et les autres signes;	 And you should know the duration of the abscess perforation according to its completion, and it is when the pain is alleviated, and the disappearance of fever, and the decrease in pain and redness, and the subsiding and shrinking of the head of the abscess, and other signs;
et covient que tu faices seoir la perforation ou plus dependant leu de l’aposteme, et la ou il apert mues;	 And you should have the perforation sit lower or depending on the abscess, and where it has begun to open.
et soit li perforation dou lonc dou cors, et se li apostemes est as mains ou as piez, ou en jointures et au ners et as arteres, et en toz leus igalz ou il n’a point de ploieure.	 And the perforation should be long along the body, and if the abscess is in the hands or feet, or in joints and nerves and arteries, and everywhere equal or without any cover.
En ces que ploient, par selonc celui membre.	 In those that are swollen, according to the affected member.
Et quant apostemes est en leu charnut, si vaut mues que tu laisses la perforation tant qu’il soit confermez en digestion acomplie, si com nos avons dit.	 And when an abscess is in a charred place, it is good to leave the perforation until it is confirmed in completed digestion, as we have said.
Car se tu lou perces devant ceu, si iert alongiez li cors dou venim de lui, et est plains de mout d’ordure;	 If you pierce through the lung before the chest, it will fill with blood and become full of filth.
et par aventure endurcissent les levres et li parfondetez de lui.	 And by chance harden the lips and push them inside him.
Et si a aucun aposteme que sont perciet selonc le large dou cors, selonc ceu que li membres en ait mestier.	 And if any abscess that has been pierced according to the size of the body, as required by the limbs.
Et covient que tu amenistres em petis apostemes, petis pertus;	 You must make small abscesses, small wounds.
et en grans apostemes, grans pertus, et maintes fendures selonc la semblance de la grandor de l’aposteme;	 and in large abscesses, large wounds, and many cuts according to the size of the abscess.
et si a de tels apostemes ou il covient chever lou keur, et coper;	 And if there are such abscesses where it is necessary to cover and keep warm.
quant il est jai devenus ausi com I drapelz, et est amortis, si covient faire ausi com on fait as bubes:	 When it has become like a scab and become soft, if it is necessary, do as for babies:
et si a de telz que sont fendut en III angles, et si a de telz dont on cope ausi com la fuelle de mirte, si com apostemes des angres;	 And if they are of such that are split into three angles, and if they are of such from which one strikes as the prickles of myrtle, like abscesses in the joints;
et si a de telz ou on fait une reonde taille, et autres tailles et semblant copeure.	 And if they are of such where a round incision is made, and other incisions and similar strikes.
Cil qui n’ont point de chief, si com aposteme souef superficial, il covient que tu lou perces plainnement;	 Those who have no head, like a superficial abscess, it is necessary that you pierce it completely;
et covient quant li apostemes est gros, et il a coillit grant bowe, et tu lou perces, si ne traire mie toute la bowe en celle houre, mais en trai une partie;	 And when the abscess is large and it has collected much pus, and you pierce it, do not draw out all the pus in that hour, but draw out a part of it;
puis estoupe l’aposteme jusc’a l’autre jor, puis en trai aucune chose derechief;	 Then stop up the abscess until the next day, then draw anything straight from it;
fai ceu par maintes fois de greit en greit, tant que li bowe isse toute;	 Make it multiple times with great effort, until the bowel is empty.
meismement se li malaides est de foible vertut, ou femme portans, ou petis enfes, ou viez hons decrepites.	 for weak patients, women, or children, or old men in decline.
Car li esperis tressaut aucune fois avec l’issue de la bowe, que par aventure muert li malaides, et tu ne t’en persois.	 The pus jumps out at times with the release of the pus, by chance the patient may die, and you should not worry.
Eschuez donques cest chapistre par grant cautele, et quant tu as perciet ton aposteme, si essue la plaie, et regarde se li plaie de l’aposteme est petite;	 Therefore, beware of this chapter with great caution, and when you have pierced the abscess, if you rinse the wound, look to see if the wound from the abscess is small.
et se c’est une tailleure plainne, si amenistre tentes de lin ou de viez coton;	 and if it is a large swelling, then bring linen or old cotton threads;
et se c’est uns grans apostemes, et il i a mout de pertus, si covient que tu boutes en chescun une tente si qu’ele viegne l’une contre l’autre;	 and if it is a large abscess and there is much pus, then you must place a thread in each one so that they come against each other;
et se tu as copeit en l’aposteme une partie dou cuir, et tu l’as cheveit entor, si covient que tu l’emplisses de viel couton ou de rasure de dras de lin sens moistor, et le lie jusc’au tier jor;	 and if you have cut into the abscess part of the skin, and you have shaved it around, then you must fill it with old cotton or raw linen wool without moisture, and tie it up for three days.
puis l’oste, et le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then bone it, and cure with ointment until it heals.
Et se decorremens de sanc avient a ton ovraige, si amenistre aigue froide et aisil, et moille I drapeil, et met sor le leu decorrant par maintes fois.	 And if bleeding occurs in your work, bring cold water and linen cloth, dampen it, and place it on the wound repeatedly.
Et se li decorremens de sanc persevere, se i amenistre governement et cure, et les poudres que j’ai dit em mains leus en cest livre, et se c’est ou tens d’iver, et li leus ou li apostemes est est mout nervous, si couvient que tu mettes sus tentes et drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile chaut;	 If the discharge of blood persists, provide management and care, and the powders that I have mentioned in this book, and if it is near winter, and the limbs or abscesses are very nervous, then you must place warm blankets soaked in hot wine and oil on top.
et se c’est en esteit, et li leus est charnus, si covient que tu mes sus drapelz moilliez en aigue et en oile, ou en vin et en oile froit, jusc’au tier jor, si com nos avons dit;	 and if it is in summer, and the limbs are fleshy, then you must place cold blankets soaked in water and oil, or in cold wine and oil for three days as we have said.
et puis deslie l’aposteme et l’essue et le cure, si com il covient, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then drain the abscess and let it heal, as necessary, until it heals.
Et ceu covient il conoistre universement en cures des apostemes:	 And this must be universally known in the treatment of abscesses:
or vos ai dit coment on doit aler avant as cures des apostemes, et vez ci le chapistre.	 or I have told you how one should proceed before the treatment of abscesses, and here is the chapter.
des soros	on les doibt traiter par cautere de feu, et si c'est li soros qui est gros ou si c'est en estete, il faut les fistraire ou les aignorer avant; et s'il sont durs et ne puissent pas fistreier, alors les coupez en peus et empoignez le tueu par dessous la poix, et mettez feu au cautere, et on les brande comme il se peut, et ains qu'il soit bien chauffez, pesez le cautere et mettez l'en une vase d'eau, et le tirez hors du tueu qui est oste; et lors que li soros seront toutes ensemeies, si les clavetiez ains qu'il se refroidissent, si com il covient.
Ou keur dou chief vienent petis apostemes, et sont manieres de nous que sont en toiles, ausi com li josier d’une geline, et mout en i a de semblances.	 For small abscesses on the head, it is our practice to use linen cloths, as a gardener with a gourd, and there are many similarities.
Il en i a de gras et de telz ou il a moistor ausi com poulz;	 There are some that are swollen and filled with moisture like boils:
et si a de telz qui sont dur et pierous au taillier, et n’i a point de doutance se li artere n’i fait contraire.	 and there are those that are hard and stony at the base, and there is no doubt that the artery does not oppose.
Et li ovraiges de la taille si est que tu esprueve a tout I estrument qui est apelez «entromissoire», de coi li forme vient ci aprés, quel chose il contient.	 And the work of cutting is that you probe with every instrument called "entomoisoir," which gives rise to the following form, what it contains.
Car s’il contient moistor, si lou fent par desus dou lonc.	 For if it contains moisture, they make a long incision through it.
Et quant li moistor est vuidie, si escorche sens rien laissier la peil qui contient celle moistor, car il revient adés quant on i laisse rien;	 When the moisture is evacuated, if you incise without leaving any skin that contains the moisture, because it will return immediately when left unattended;
puis plonge coton en oignement egiptien, s’il est presens;	 then immerse cotton in Egyptian oil if it is available:
se ceu non, en aigue et en seil, et en emple la plaie, et la laisse jusc’a l’autre jor;	 if not, use water and salt, and apply the wound, and leave it until the next day:
et ceu corront ceu qui est demorez dou nit.	 And these (things) move those who have remained (stuck) at night.
Et pues rencomence lou coton, si com devant, le second jor, et lou tier, tant que tu saiches bien qu’il ne demoure point dou nit;	 And renew the cotton, as before, on the second day and the third, until you know that it does not remain at night.
puis cure la plaie d’oignement a ceu convenauble, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then heal the wound with ointment as appropriate, until it is healed.
Et se li apostemes tient I nout gras, si le cope selonc ceste forme, dou lonc;	 And if the abscess remains filled with fat, flatten it according to this shape, longwise;
et i giete tes oncines, et l’escorche de toutes pars, et met toute ta cure de traire fuer la cotte ou il gist;	 and pour out the pus, and peel off all of it from every side, and put your entire treatment to draw fire through the coat in which it lies.
et se li artere te fait contraire, si fai ceu que je t’ai dit aprés.	 And if the arteries oppose you, do what I have said after.
Et ausi fai de l’aposteme s’il est pierous, et dou taillier et dou curer si com je t’ai dit.	 And similarly do for the abscess if it is pockmarked, and cut and treat as I told you before.
Et li taille sus l’aposteme pierous et le moiste, si est plus legiere, car il sont de poc de sanc.	 And the incision on the abscess becomes moist, it is lighter, for there is little blood.
Et si a aucuns de ces apostemes ou chief ou il n’a point de moistor, et de ces fut I apostemes que je copai ou chief d’une vielle femme;	 And if any of these abscesses or head has no moisture, and these are the abscesses that I flattened on the head of an old woman;
et trovai l’aposteme ausi com une piere xourde, aspre et blainche, et ne pooit brisier;	 And I found the abscess just like a hard and swollen stone, unbreakable.
et s’on en eust ferut aucun, on li eust ausi bien fait plaie com d’une piere.	 And if one had pierced it with anything, it would have made as much wound as a stone.
En autres apostemes venans ou chief, fuer que ces qui vienent as chief des enfans et as racines des oreilles, li overture si soit toz jors au plus dependant leu, por mues issir la bowe;	 In other abscesses coming from the head, such as those that come from a child's head or the roots of the ears, they must be opened for as long as possible depending on their location, to allow the pus to flow out.
et les cure si com il covient.	 and they are treated as needed.
des scrophules	of scrofulas
Maintes fois avienent cist aposteme au col, et desoz les asseles, et ens angres, et aucune fois vienent autre part ou cors, et sont mout, et sont enjanrees l’une avec l’autre.	 Often this abscess occurs at the neck, under the jaw, and in the groin area, and sometimes it appears elsewhere on the body, and they are large and connected to each other.
Et chescune scrophule est proprement dedens sa cote, si com li nout et li aposteme dou chief, si com nos avons dit;	 And each scrofula is properly within its own side, like the abscess of the head, as we have said.
et les semblances de ces scrophules sont maintes.	 The resemblance of these scrofulas are many.
Il i a de teles que contienent moistor, et si a de malignes qui ne vuellent obeir a santeit.	 There are some that contain moisture, and others that are malicious and do not want to obey health.
en celle donques que tu vois de bone disposition au tochier, et est semblans a la color dou cors, et muet de chescune part et n’est mie aerse as ners dou col ne a l’artere ne au conduit, et n’est mie parfonde;	 In that case, you see it in good position on the body, and resembles the color of the body, silent from all sides and not pulsating at the neck or artery or vein, and is not deep.
si covient que tu la copes par desus, et l’escorche de chescune partie, et estent les II levres dou keur as oncines, se tu en as mestier, si com nos avons dit en apostemes dou chief;	 You must cut it through the top, and peel off each part, and hold open the two lips of the incision with forceps, if necessary, as we have said in abscesses of the head.
et la trai poc et poc, et soies seur que tu ne coper lou nerf ne la voine, et ne soit mie li spatumile agus ne trenchans, que li mains n’eschaipe, et ne voise trop avant, que tu ne coper mie ceu que tu ne dois.	 pull it slowly and be sure not to cut the nerve or vein, and may the spatula not touch nor scratch, so that the hand does not slip, and look not too far ahead, lest you cut what you should not.
Et se tu copes la voinne ou l’artere, et ceu ne te laisse ovrer, si met en la plaie vitriole broiet, ou aucunes poudres que restainchent sanc, et estraint la plaie;	 And if you open the vein or artery and it does not yield, put vitriol powder into the wound or any powders that stop blood, and hold the wound closed.
et la laisse tant que li apostemes soit apaisiez, et soit amollie li plaie, et encomence a porrir.	 And let the abscess be appeased, and soften the wound, and make it start to drain.
Et quant li sans est estainchiez, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que tu l’acomplisses;	 And when the blood has stopped flowing, return to your work until you finish.
puis quier a ton doit indice s’il i demoure nules petites scrophules, si les cope et les munde.	 Then examine if there are any small scrofulas remaining, and if so, cut them out and clean them.
Et s’il a en la racine de la scrophule voinne grant, si ne covient mie que tu copes celle scrophule en sa racine, mais la lie d’un fil double fort, et la laisse cheoir par li, sens nuisement;	 If the root of the scrofula has a large vein, it is not necessary to cut out that scrofula at its root, but tie it with a strong doubled thread and let it hang down without harm.
puis emple la plaie de viel coton plongiet en oignement egiptien, puis la cure.	 Then apply the wound with old cotton dipped in Egyptian ointment, then let it heal.
Et se tu copes toute la scrophule, si covient que tu assembles les II levres de la plaie, et les cout maintenant, puis qu’il n’i a point demoreit de superfluiteit por la grandor de la scrophule.	 And if you excise the entire scrofula, it is necessary that you close the two lips of the wound, and sew them now, since there is no more superfluous material remaining due to the largeness of the scrofula.
si covient que tu entendes a coper la racine de li, et traire fuer, et la cout si com nos avons dit.	 It is necessary that you understand to cover the root of it and draw pus, and sew it as we have said.
Celles scrophules que tienent superfluiteit, perce lai ou il apert meure;	 Those scrofulas that have excess fluid, pierce there where it has burst open;
et la perce ensi com celle devant dite, en dependant, puis i amenistre tentes avec oignement et semblans choses, si qu’elle corrompe ceu qui est demorez de la corruption;	 and pierce in the same way as described before, depending on it, then apply poultices with ointment and similar things, so that it corrodes what remains of the corruption;
et quant li plaie est bien mundee, si la cure d’oignement enjanrant char, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And when the wound is well cleaned, let it heal with bright ointment, until it is healed.
de squinance	If you make a bloodletting from the artery, then you must bind the veins that are near so that the bleeding does not continue, and close the wound with clean cloths.
Li ancien dirent et parlerent de la tailleure de la gorge;	 The ancients spoke of the shape of the throat;
mais je ne vis onques en nostre terre qui la feist, et c’est li escripture de lor parole.	 But I have never seen one who did it in our land, and it is written in their words.
A ces qui ont squinance, il covient que li fendure de la gorge qui est apelee «epiglote» soit eschuee;	 For those who have scinases (a term likely referring to goiter), it is necessary that the cleft in the throat called "epiglottis" be shaved.
et c’on ne faice aide par ceu, por ceu que toutes les voines et li pormon dou malaide sont a ces qui ont aposteme chaut en la bouche, ou en la gorge ou en II amandres.	 And do not help with that, because all the veins and the swelling of the patient are in those who have an abscess hot in the mouth or in the throat or in both cheeks.
Quant li maladie est en la chenal dou pormon, il covient coper l’epiglote por fuir la perdition qui vient de l’estranglement.	When the sickness is in the channel of the tonsil, it is required to cover the epiglottis to avoid the danger that comes from strangulation.
Il covient donques, quant nos volons fendre l’epiglote, que nos le fendons desoz III cercles ou IIII une petite fendure dou travers, entre les II cercles ou par la quantiteit de la fendure dou syfac, ne mie en la cartillaige;	 Therefore, when we want to cut the epiglottis, it is necessary that we make the incision below three or four small circles or a small slit across, between the two circles or through the thickness of the incision due to the scissors, not in the cartilage.
et cil leus si est covenaubles a la section de l’epiglote qu’il n’i a point de char, et li vasseil sont lonc d’enqui.	 And the patients who are subjected to the incision of the epiglottis should not have any cartilage, and the veins are long in length.
Et se li maistres est paourous, si covient qu’il estende le cuir de la gorge a tout l’oncine, puis fende lou keur tant qu’il viegne a la cheneil;	 And if the master is afraid, he must stretch the skin of the throat all the way to the chin, then cut open the breast until it reaches the cartilage;
et eschue les vasselz de sanc, se tu vois aucune chose, et puis cope lou syfac, si com nos avons dit;	 and remove any vessels of blood that you see, and then press the siphac as we have said;
et est demostrez par la section dou fleume de la cheneil ki saut fuer par le leu qui est rompus, et par la defaute de la voix;	 and demonstrated by the section of the breastbone that juts out due to the broken place, and by the lack of voice;
et laisse la plaie overte une piece.	 leave the wound open for a while.
Et quant li houre est passee de coi on doute l’estranglement, assemble les II levres de la plaie dou keur, et la cout toute soule sens la cartillaige;	 And when the hour has passed in doubt of strangulation, bring together the two edges of the wound from the breastbone and sew it completely closed around the cartilage;
puis aministre medicines qui font naistre char, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 then administer medicines that cause pus to form until it is healthy.
Albucasim dist c’on ne faice ce jusc’a tant que li gorge est toute estoupee, et li malaides est jugiez a mort, et li defaut li alaine.	Abu'l-Qasim says not to do this until the throat is completely stopped up, and the patient is judged dead, and the bird pecks out his eyes.
Adonques cope on l’epiglote por ceu que li malaides ne puet alener, et il respire par la plaie, et ensi est gardez de mort;	 Therefore, press on the epiglottis because the patient cannot swallow, and he breathes through the wound, thus keeping him alive.
et por ce commanderent li anciain a laissier la plaie overte tant que li malice de la maladie soit passee, et elle est passee en III jors ou en IIII Et adonques il comanderent a coudre la plaie et curer, tant qu’elle fut curee;	 And so, the ancients would leave the wound open until the evil of the disease had passed, which it had done in three or four days, and then they would command to sew up the wound and heal it.
et je vos dirai ceu que je vis.	 And I will tell you what I have seen.
Je vis que une damoisele prist I coutel, et le ficha en sa gorge, et copa partie des chenelz dou pormon;	 I saw a maiden take the knife, thrust it into her throat, and cut part of the windpipe channels.
et je fui apelez por li curer, et la trovai ausi com morte.	 And I was called to heal her, and found her in the same state as death.
Je descovris la plaie, et trovai le sanc qui en estoit issus, et soi bien qu’elle n’avoit mie copeit voine ne conduit fuer que la gorge, et li vens issoit fuer par la plaie.	I found the wound and discovered blood coming out of it, and that it had not opened or led the vein except through the throat, and the veins were flowing through the wound.
Je me hastai, et cousi la plaie, et la curai tant qu’elle fut sanee;	 I hastily sewed up the wound, healed it until it was cured;
et n’avint a la damoisele fuer qu’elle fut roge de voix, et revint aprés a sa disposition;	 And there was no more pain to the maiden except she became red of voice, and she returned afterwards to her condition.
por ceu di je que en la tailleure de l’epiglote n’ait mie paour.	 For this reason, I say that in the case of the epiglottis there should be no fear.
de la grosse gorge	of the large throat
Cist apostemes est apelez «hernie de gorge», et est uns grans apostemes en color d’une jaisse, et est molt en femmes;	 This abscess is called "throat hernia" and it is a large abscess of the color of a pigeon's breast, and it is often in women.
et est selonc II manieres:	 and it can occur in two ways:
naturez, et accidens;	 Nature and accidents.
ou natureil n’a point d’engien.	 Nature has no trickery.
Et li accidens est selonc II manieres, de coi l’une est semblans a gras nous, et li autre maniere est semblans a aposteme qui vient de nous d’artere;	 And accidents are of two kinds, one is like fatness in us, and the other kind is similar to an abscess that comes from us due to an artery.
et il i ait paour, et ne covient mie ovrer de feir fuers que en celi qui est petite, et le prueve et cerche a tout l’intromissoire:	 And there is fear, and it should not be operated on harshly except in the case of a small one; prove and examine all through the incision:
se tu le trueves ausi com I nout gras, et ne pent a nulle voine, si le cope, si com on cope les nous, et le trai a tout sa coife, s’il en i a point;	 If you find it as if fat, and it cannot move in any way, strike it like one strikes the nose, and pull it out completely, if there is anything;
et encerche bien tot, et le cure si com il covient, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	 And examine carefully, and heal it as needed, until it is perfectly healed.
des nous	from us
Maintes manieres de nous sont, dont je dirai toutes les semblances;	 Many ways of ours are, which I shall say all similarities;
et or covient que je die toute la difference qui est entre nout et issue.	 and it is necessary that I say the whole difference that is between joint and dislocation.
Je dis que issue est chalors et fievre tenans, tant que li ebulicions est passee, et est acomplie li porriture;	 I say that dislocation is hot and fever lasting, until the boil has passed, and the swelling has subsided.
adonques repose li fievre et li chalor.	 then the fever and heat subside.
Avec lou nout n’a ne chalor ne fievre ne dolor, et contient I syfac, qui est ses propres sac et est selonc la color dou cors, et encomence ausi com une jaisse, et devient gros;	 With the joint there is no heat, no fever, nor pain, and it contains the pus, which is its own sack and is according to the color of the body, and begins like a blister, and grows.
et sont selonc II semblances, ou grais, ou moiste, et mout de color sont si com j’ai dit en la division.	 and they are similar in one way or another, either thickened, moist, and have much of the same color as I have said in the divisions.
Il covient, quant tu viens a la cure dou nout, que tu esprueves et l’enquier premierement a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «entromissoire», selonc ce que sa forme venra ou chapistre qui est aprés.	It is necessary when you come to the care of the sick, that you examine and test first all the instruments called "entromissoire," according to its shape or chapter that follows.
Et li maniere de l’inquisicion des apostemes des nous est que tu preignes ou plus moiste leu que tu trueves en l’aposteme, et torne tes dois poc et poc, tant que tu saiches que li estrumens ait perciet le keur, puis que ce soit selonc la grandor de l’aposteme;	 And the method of incising abscesses for us is that you take or more moist leather than you find in the abscess, and turn your thumbs little by little, until you know that the instrument has pierced through, then it should be according to the size of the abscess;
puis estrai l’entromissoire, et pren garde en ceu que saut fuer.	 Then extract the incision tool, and take care that it does not come out.
Se moistor corrans cort, queil color elle ait, si le fent si com j’ai dit des autres apostemes;	 If moisture runs out, that it has colored [the abscess], do as I have said about other abscesses;
et se aprés l’entromissoire nen vient moistor, saiches qu’il est gras, si le fent donques en croix, et le prent as pinceures, et l’escorche legierement de chescune part et warde la cotte ou il gist que tu la traies saine avec le nout;	 And if after the incision tool no moisture comes out, know that it is fat, then do it in crossways, take hold of it with the tweezers and lightly peel it from both sides and ward the coat where it lies so you draw it out whole with the sinew.
et se tu ne la pues traire saine, si la trai par pieces si qu’il n’i demoure rien.	 If you cannot draw it safely, draw it in parts so that nothing remains.
Car s’il i demoure rien, si revient li nous par maintes fois;	 For if something remains, it will return to us many times;
et s’il en demore un poc, et li sans te grieve, si emple la plaie d’aucunes poudres corrosives agues, et estraint la plaie, et met sus choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	 If a small amount remains and does not cause you grief, apply some corrosive powders to the wound, hold the wound together, cover it with warm soothing substances, and treat it with other treatments until it heals.
et se li nous est grans, si cout les II levres de la plaie, et le cure de ceu qui enjanre char.	 If it is large, cut the wound into two lips, and heal it with flesh-growing agents.
et se li voine batans t’est contraire ou autre si te haste et emple le leu de vitriole broiet, et lou laisse liiet II jors ou III, tant que li plaie porrisse, et repose li ebulicion dou sanc;	 If the veins beating against you or someone else hurries and you use glass powder, leave it lying for 2 or 3 days until the wound festers, and let the boiling of blood subside;
puis revien au coper ceu que i est demoreit dou nout.	 Then return to bind what has been left unbound with sutures.
Vez ci les formes des estrumens entromissoires, et sont de III manieres:	 Here are the shapes of cutting instruments and they come in three kinds:
grans et moien et petit;	 large, medium, and small;
et s’en i a III quarrez qui sont apelez «albaret», et I qui est apelez «breb», et s’en i a de III manieres:	 And there are three squares, which are called "albarets", and one that is called "breb", and there are three ways of it:
grant, moien, et petit, por encerchier les apostemes de fistule;	 Large, medium, and small, to surround the abscesses with fistulas.
et sont ausi com les aguilles dont on cout les sorceles, et sont d’arain citrin, ou de fer, ou d’argent, et mues valent cil qui sont jaune, et sont plus esprovez de plonc noir por encerchier les corbeures de fistule;	 and they are like needles with which witches are sewn, and they are made of citron wood, or iron, or silver, and yellow ones are valued more, and black ones are more proven to surround the swellings of a fistula.
et sont de III manieres:	 There are three kinds of them:
grans, moiens, et petis, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce des pertus.	 large, medium, and small, according to the width of the wounds.
Les formes des oncines sont de mout de semblances, si com tu vois ci:	 The shapes of the funnels are similar to one another, as you see here:
grans, moiens, et petis;	 Large, medium, and small.
et si a oncines qui ont II corbeures de III manieres ausi;	 And if the ones with two humps have three shapes as well;
et si a oncines qui ont III corbeures, et sont ausi de III manieres;	 And if the ones with three humps have three shapes, and are also of three kinds.
et si a oncines qui ont II corbeures, et oncines d’une corbeure soulement, et sont de III manieres;	 And if the ones with two humps have one hump only, and the ones with one hump are of three kinds.
et tuit cist sont necessaire en lor leu.	 And all these are necessary in their place.
Li chief de ces a coi on fent sont trenchant, et de telz i a qui ne taillent mie fuer que d’une part, dont on escorche les nous, por ceu c’on ne cope la voine ne le nerf;	 The main ones with which we perform this are sharp, and of those who do not cut at all except from one side, for we scrape the nails with them, so as not to strike the vein or the nerve.
et de ces intromissoires sont les alemeles reponues en mainches, si que li malaide ne s’en persoivent a l’overture des apostemes;	 And of these probing instruments, the needles are tied in bunches so that the patient does not prick themselves at the opening of abscesses.
et sont de III manieres:	 And there are three kinds:
grant, petit, et moien, si com tu vois;	 large, small, and medium, as you can see;
et n’en use on mie fuer que en leu charnut, si com jambes, et bras, et mameles, et as angres, et en semblans leus;	 do not use them in any other place except for the chest (ribs), like legs, arms, breasts, and ankles, and similar places.
et aucune fois fait on I autre estrument petit, semblant a escorces de fistices, selonc ceste forme, a coi on estainche sanc:	 Sometimes another small instrument similar to fistulae scissors is used in this way to draw blood.
et le met on aucune fois au leu qui saine a copement des voines, et as arteres, et aucune fois reont selonc ceste grant forme:	and it is put to the place that stops bleeding from veins, arteries, and sometimes returns according to this large shape:
Aucune fois enflent les mameles d’aucuns homes quant cil encomencent estre corrumput, tant qu’eles semblent mameles de feme;	 Sometimes the breasts of some men swell when they begin to become corrupt, until they resemble female breasts.
et demorent laides et enflees, et qui les vuet curer, si le covient soier selonc ceste forme des ceste ligne .b. jusques a .g.:	 and remain ugly and swollen, and whoever wishes to treat them should do it according to this form from line b to g:
puis escorche la graisse, et emple la plaie de medicine enjanrant char, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie a costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee;	 then cut the fat, apply medicine to the wound containing burnt charcoal, then close the two lips of the wound with stitches, and treat it until it is healed.
et se li mamele cline aval, et est amolie por sa grandor si com il avient as femmes, si la fent en II costelz desus, par II semblans fendures;	 And if the arm is bent downward and flattened due to its size, as happens with women, then it should be split into two halves, through two similar-looking cracks.
de coi l’une soit tenans a l’autre a la fin de l’une et de l’autre, si que li plus grans ligne conteigne la menor selonc ceste forme, des ceste ligne .b. jusc’a la ligne .g.;	 so that one remains attached to the other at the end of one and the other, so that the larger line contains the smaller according to this shape, from this line b to line g;
puis escorche le cuir qui est entre les II levres, et oste la graisse, et i amenistre ceu que nos avons dit de costure et de poudres, et ceu qui est necessaire en la cure, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 then peel the skin between the two jaws, remove the fat, and bring what we have said about stitching and powders, and whatever is necessary for treatment, until it heals.
et s’il n’est sanez, ou li incision n’est mie toute faite, por ceu que li malaides ne vuet reposer, ou por le decorrement de sanc, si covient que tu emplisses la plaie de coton moilliet en oignement corrosif;	 if it is not healed or the incision is not completely made because the patient does not want to rest, or due to bleeding, then you must fill the wound with moistened cotton in a corrosive ointment.
et le laisse tant qu’il menjuce le remenant et la graisse, puis le cure tant qu’il soit saneis.	 And leave it until it consumes the remaining meat and fat, then heal it until it is healed.
des apostemes des asselles	From abscesses of buttocks
Cist apostemes que vienent desoz les asseles sont manieres de scrophules dures ou il ait cotes, et s’en i a que contienent moistor.	These abscesses that come from the buttocks are cases of hard scrofula where there is moisture contained within them.
Cil donques qui contienent moistor covient qu’il soient copez selonc ceste forme, des la ligne .b. jusc’a la ligne .g.:	 Therefore, those who contain moisture should be cut according to this form, from the line 'b' up to the line 'g': [This part doesn't need translation as it is a technical instruction about making a surgical cut.]
Et quant toute li bowe qui est en l’aposteme est vuidie, si emple la plaie de viel coton, et la laisse jusc’a l’autre jor, puis oste tout le coton, et cure d’oignement avenant a ceu tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when the entire bowel in the abscess is emptied, fill the wound with old cotton and leave it until the next day, then remove all the cotton and treat it with ointment until it heals.
Et se li apostemes est de semblances de scrophules, si le fent si com nos avons dit en fendures des scrophules, et se li plaie rent bowe, si amenistre cautere si com nos avons dit devant.	And if the abscess resembles scrofula (or scrofulous lesions), then make incisions in it as we have said before in scrofula incisions, and if the wound swells, apply a cautery as we have said before.
de la routure de l’artere	The cutting of an artery.
Quant li artere est route, et li cuir est soudez qui est sus, si en vient maintes fois apostemes, et tout aussi avient il a la voine enflee et aposteme;	 When an artery is ruptured and the skin above it is stuck together, there are often abscesses, and the same happens with an inflamed vein and abscess.
et si le conoist on ensi quant c’est por l’artere, si est li apostemes lons em parfont;	 And if it is recognized in such a way that it is due to an artery, the abscess is long and deep.
et quant tu le sens a tes dois, si sens I estraignement;	 And when you feel it with your hand, you should stretch it.
et quant c’est por la voine, si est reons defuer aparans;	 And when it is the vein, it feels shallow and round.
et c’est folie de coper cest aposteme, et meismement quant il est desoz les asseles et as angres et ou col et em mout d’autres leus, et est mout grans.	 It is foolish to cover this abscess, and especially when it is under the armpit and near the joints or neck and in other places, and is very large.
Il covient donques eschuir la cure de fer, et celui qui est a chief covient eschuir ausi, et en celui qui est d’enfleure d’artere fent par desus le cuir dou lonc;	 Therefore, it is necessary to avoid iron treatment, and the same goes for those with head injuries, and in the case of a swelling from an artery, they should be cut through the skin on top.
puis oevre la taille as oncines, et depart bellement l’artere des toiles, tant qu’ele soit descoverte;	 Then open the groin area, and carefully disconnect the artery from the fabrics, until it is exposed.
