puis boute desoz li une aguille, et la fai percier jusc’a l’autre costeit, et estraint l’artere d’un fil double en II leus, selonc ceu que je t’ai ensigniet en l’estraction des II arteres qui sont en temples;	 Then insert an awl underneath it and make it pierce until the other side, and tie the artery with a double thread in two places, as I have taught you in the extraction of the two arteries that are in the temples.
puis point le leu qui est entre les II liens d’un intromissoire tant que li sans en isse qui i est, et soit deliiez li aposteme;	 Then prick the place between the two ligatures with a probe until the abscess comes out.
puis amenistre la cure que enjanre bowe, tant que li liien chient;	 Then apply the cure by clamping a splint, as long as the limb cries out.
puis cure ceu d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 Then apply the cure with soothing ointment until it is healed;
et se li apostemes est por la taille de la voinne, si covient que tu teignes a ta main ceu que tu pues de l’aposteme a tout le cuir, puis boute l’aguille desoz le leu que tu tiens a ta main, et la fai percier, et i ait I fil double, si que tu le trais de l’autre costeit;	 And if the abscess is due to the opening of a vein, you must anoint your hand with what you can from the abscess all over the skin, then put the needle under the place that you hold in your hand and make it pierce through, and have double thread so you can draw it from the other side.
puis lie l’aposteme, si com je t’ai dit, ou liien de l’une de II pars as II chiés dou fil;	 Then tie the abscess, as I told you, or bind one of its parts with two threads around the two shoulders.
et se tu doutes que li filz n’isse fuer, si i reboute une autre aguille a tout I fil desoz tout l’aposteme a l’incision de la premiere aguille, et estraint les filz en IIII leus;	 And if you doubt that the thread has gone through, push another needle all along the length of the abscess at the incision of the first needle, and tighten the threads in four places.
puis cope l’aposteme tant que li superfluitez en isse, puis cope la superfluiteit dou keur et laisse ceu qui est liiez;	 Then press the abscess until the pus comes out, then press the cavity and leave what is tied.
puis met sus I drapeil moilliet en vin et en oile, puis li amenistre cures de tentes et d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then place a damp cloth soaked in wine and oil on it, then treat it with bandages and salves until it heals.
des apostemes des ners	from abscesses of nerves
Ausi com aposteme vienent en l’artere et en la voine, vienent aposteme as ners quant il sont ferut, ou par trop grant travail, et semblans choses.	Just like abscesses can occur in the artery and vein, so too do abscesses come to the nerves when they are injured or from excessive labor, and similar things.
Et ceu avient plus sovent as adjutoires et as dois et en toz leus ou il ait jointures, et c’est I grief apostemes, et sa color semble la color dou cors, et est em plusors dispositions sens dolor;	 This happens more often in shoulders and fingers and all places where there are joints, and it is the greatest abscess, and its color resembles the body's color, and it is found in various positions with pain.
et quant on l’estraint forment, si sent li malaides dolor, et n’est mie em parfont dou cors, mais desoz lou keur;	 And when it is squeezed, the patient feels pain, but it is not at the skin level, but beneath the flesh.
et muet bien de toutes pars, et ne va ne avant ne arrier, ne desoz ne desus, et celui qui est en jointures ne covient mie coper par fer:	 It should be bound from all sides, and it does not move forward or backward, nor below nor above; the one in a joint should not be treated with iron.
par aventure i vanroit contraction;	 By chance, it may come to contraction;
et cil qui est ou chief ou ou front, fent le cuir au spatumile.	 And whoever is [either] head or forehead, [should make] the skin with a spatula.
Se li apostemes est petis, si le tien a unes tenailles, et le cope en sa racine;	 If the abscess is small, hold it with tweezers and strike at its root;
et s’il est grans, si le sospent a l’oncine, et l’escorche, puis l’oste et assemble la plaie a la costure, et lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 If it is large, suspend it on the incision, and strip it, then cut and close the wound at the suture, and the cure until it heals.
des grosses boces pendans	Large lumps hanging
Aucune fois avient en ventres et ne mie autre part thelul, et est une maladie qui est apelee «funge» par la semblance d’aus, et est li racine subtilz, et li chiez gros;	 Sometimes it happens in bellies and nowhere else, and it is a disease called "fungus" due to its resemblance [to mushrooms], and the roots are subtle, and the heads large;
et en i a de petis et de mout grans;	 and there are some small ones and very large ones;
et je vis I home qui en avoit II ou ventre qui estoient plus semblans a funges que ai autre chose, et n’i avoit point de difference, et estoient blanc, et avoient menue racine, et estoient jai fendut, et en corroit adés moistor.	 And I saw a man who had two bellies that resembled mushrooms more than anything else, and there was no difference between them, and they were white, and had small roots, and were cut open, and continually oozed moisture.
Je les copai et trovai en l’un XVIII onces pesant, et en l’autre VI З., et li ovraiges en l’incision si est que tu regardes se li malaides est moistes, et li color de l’artelul est blainche et moiste et de subtil racine;	 I weighed them and found one to be 18 ounces, the other 6, and the wounds in the incision were such that you can see if the patient is moist, and the color of the artery is pale and moist with a thin root.
si le cope au spatumile large, et soient en ta presence li cautere au feu.	 If you cut it with a broad spatula, let the fire cautery be present.
Car au taillier vient maintes fois trop grans decorremens de sanc, et se li sans te vaint, si te haste donques dou cauterizer;	 For during the dissection there are often excessive bleeding, and if it threatens you, quickly use the cautery.
et se tu vois le malaide espoanteit et paourous de l’incision dou fer, si prent I fil de plonc bien fait, et en lie l’artelul si com nos avons dit, et le laisse II jors;	 And if you see the patient fearful and afraid of the incision with iron, take a well-made thread, and tie the artery as we have said, and leave it for two days;
et puis le restraint, et ne cesser d’estraindre lou fil de plonc tant qu’il cope l’artelul, et chiece par lui sens travail;	 Then hold it tight, and do not stop tightening the thread of flax until it stops the artery flow, and he feels labor pains.
et se les racines sont grosses, si a paour au coper meismement por le ventre, mais tu em pues bien coper la moitiet, puis le cauterize qu’il ne reviegne;	 If the roots are large, he is afraid to press himself because of his stomach, but you can cover half of it, then burn it so it does not return.
puis cure la plaie, et garde que tu ne coper le thelul qui est de fuxe color et de povre sens et de lait regart.	 Then heal the wound, and ensure that you do not cover the thread that is of a dark color and poor quality and milky appearance.
Car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, et je venrai a la cure de chancre ci aprés.	For this is an enlarged abscess, and I will come to the treatment of syphilis afterward.
quant li boude ist fuer	when the boil bursts out
Se li apparance de la boude vient par cautere de plaie ou de fendure de syfac, et est sus le ventre et en ist aucuns des bouez, si com il avient en autres routures, ou de sanc qui cort de voines ou d’arteres selonc ceu qui est devant, ou de ventositeit;	 If the swelling appears due to cauterization of a wound or a cut on the face, and it is on the stomach and among some of the boils, as happens in other routes, or from blood that leaks from veins or arteries as described before, or due to inflammation;
et se c’est par la routure dou syfac et par l’issue dou bouel, si est li color de l’aposteme semblans a la color dou cors, et est legiere chose sens dolor, et apert de diverse issue.	 And if it is through the break of the shaft and the exit of the bulb, then the color of the abscess resembles the color of the body, and it is a light thing without pain, and open with various exits.
Et se c’est por l’issue de l’intestine, adonques est il plus divers, et quant on le presse a ses dois si se repont, et puis revient, et par aventure si est sarrez, et agrandist mout a l’entree dou bain et por fort travail.	If it is caused by the outburst from the intestines, then it is more various. When you press it with your hands and it recedes, it returns again, and sometimes if it is sutured, it grows greatly at the entrance of the bath and due to hard work.
Et se c’est por moistor, c’est legiere chose, et apert bien quant tu le presses a ta main, ne ne constraint mie;	 And if it's due to moisture, it is light and opens wide when you press it with your hand, do not force it.
et se c’est por sanc, si apert par ces signes li apostemes gros et dur, et est fichiez selonc une quantiteit;	 And if it's due to blood, the abscess opens with these signs: large and hard, and is filled according to a certain quantity.
et se c’est por ventositeit, si est souef au tochier, et li ovraiges si est que tu regarde se li apparance est por le sanc de l’artere, ou de la voine, ou ventositeit.	 And if it's due to ventosity (gas), it is soft to the touch, and the work is that you look to see if its appearance is due to blood from an artery or vein, or gas.
Si covient que tu laisses la cure.	 It is necessary to let the treatment rest.
Car il en a doutance et paor, si com je t’ai dit ou chapistre des apostemes, por l’artere et por la voine.	 For there is doubt and fear, as I have told you in the chapter on abscesses, concerning the artery and vein.
Et se li apparance est por l’intestine ou lou boueil, si covient que tu comandes au malaide qu’il teigne son alaine, et soit estendus tout drois, puis seigne d’enche tout entor la boude;	 And if the appearance is from the intestine or the belly, you must instruct the patient to lean their backside, and stretch out straight, then sign all around the belly.
puis le comande a gesir sovin entre tes mains, puis va entor le leu que tu as signiet a tout le spatumile, puis estent la moitiet de l’aposteme au desus a tout le grant uncine;	 Then command him to press gently between your hands, then go around the place you have signed with a small spoon, then stretch out half of the abscess above the large incision.
puis le lie entor d’un fil fort, ou d’une corde de fort soie fermement, et soit li nous dou liien assolz;	 Then tie it tightly with a strong thread or a cord of strong silk, and let the patient lean forward.
puis oevre la moitiet de l’aposteme estendut sus le liien, et i boute ton doit indice, et quier l’intestine;	 Then open half of the extended abscess tied with the thread, and put your index finger in, seeking the intestine.
se tu le trueves pris dou liien, si le deslie, et boute l’intestine au defuer dou ventre;	 If you find it caught by the cord, untie it, and push the intestine out of the abdomen.
et se tu trueves le boueil, si le prent a l’oncine, et en cope la superfluiteit;	 And if you find the boil, take it at its onset, and cut off the excess.
et se li artere te fait contraire, ou li voine, si vai belement entor, puis revien a ton ovraige et pren II aguilles, et i boute II fors filz, et boute les II aguilles entor ceu que tu as fait en crois que tu feis percier;	 And if the artery becomes constricted or the vein, go gently around it, then return to your work and take two needles, and thrust two wires through them, and thrust the needles around that which you have made in a cross shape so that you pierce it.
puis estrain l’aposteme en IIII leus sus les aguilles, et se tu vues, oste les aguilles, et laisse lou leu tant qu’il porrisse, et chiece li char morte par soi;	 then press the abscess in four leagues above the needles, and if you see, remove the needles, and leave the place until it can heal by itself; the dead flesh will decay of its own accord.
ou tu la cope quant elle iert subtiliie et porrie, puis le cure de ceu qu’il covient, et cheve l’aposteme si com nos avons dit;	 or you cut it when it is soft and can be pierced, then treat it as necessary, and cover the abscess as we have said.
et estrai le sanc ou la moistor que tu trueves, puis cure le leu de ceu qu’il couvient, et soude le leu.	 Draw out the blood or moisture that you find, then heal the place as necessary, and suture the place.
dou chancre	draw the boil
Nos avons dit en la division les semblances de chancre, et coment on i doit ovrer par medicines, et coment on doit eschuer la cure de fer;	 We have stated in the preceding section the likenesses of scrofula, and how it should be treated with medicines, and how the cure of iron should be administered.
et disons le chancre enjanreit en la marris, et grant cautele a en la cure, et dirent li ancien que quant chancres est en leu ou on le puet raier si com chancre qui est em mameles, et en la cuixe, et en semblans leus, et le doit tout oster quant il est en l’encomencement;	 Now we will speak of scrofula occurring in the arm, and great caution is required in its treatment, and the ancients said that when a scrofula occurs in a place where it can be shaved like scrofula in the breast or thigh, or in similar places, it should be completely removed when it first appears.
et quant il est grans et anciens, si ne covient mie que tu l’aproches, car je n’en poi onques nul saner;	 And when it is large and old, you must not approach it, for I can never heal it.
ne nulz n’en sana onques devant moi.	 In this context, "ne nulz" means "no one", and "n'en sana onques devant moi" means "can never heal it before me". This is a continuation of the previous sentence.
Et li ovraiges, quant il est en leu ou on le puet oster, si com nos avons dit, est que tu purge aucune fois le malaide de cole noire;	 And the workings, when they are in place where they can be removed, as we have said, is that you cleanse once the sick person of black bile.
puis le fai sainier s’il ait manifeste repletion, puis afaite le malaide I boin leu por faire l’ovraige;	 then make him purge if there is manifest repletion, then prepare the patient well to perform the working.
puis giete tes oncines ou chancre, et le cheve de toutes pars, et l’oste de toutes pars sens rien laissier;	 then you throw your onions or boils and all the hair from every part, and the bone from every part leaving nothing.
et laisse corre le sanc tout fuer, et espreint bien le leu a ta main ou a aucune chose, et se li decorremens de sanc te fait contraire de l’incision de l’artere ou de la voine, si le cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	 And let the blood flow freely, press well on the spot with your hand or something, and if the movement of blood opposes the incision of an artery or vein, cauterize until the wound is coagulated.
puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then heal it from another treatment as long as it is healthy.
de ydropisie	The translation for this line would be "of hydropisia." Hydropisia refers to a medical condition in which there is excessive accumulation of water or fluid in the body tissues, specifically in the abdominal cavity.
Nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’idropisie, et en queil maniere li assemblee de l’aigue est faite, et les signes de chescune semblance, et la cure qui est faite par medicines, et cele qui est curee par fer:	 We have said in the division the resemblances of dropsy, and how its assembly is made, and the signs for each resemblance, and the medicine treatment and that which is cured by iron.
si est eclites soulement;	 if it breaks out only.
et ne doit on touchier de fer en ces II semblances:	 And one should not use iron in these two resemblances.
c’est a savoir, tympanites et yposarche, car c’est mortelz chose;	 That is to say, tympanites and hypochondriac, because it is deadly.
donques quant tu medicines ceste semblance de ydropisie qui est apelee «eclites» de medicines, et li cure ne profite, si regarde se li malaides est foibles, ou s’il ait autre maladie que ydropisie, si com toust et solution de ventre et semblans choses;	 Therefore, when you treat this appearance of edema, called "eclites," and the cure does not help, consider whether the patient is weak or if they have another disease apart from edema, such as abdominal distension and similar things.
si n’i touchier de fer, car il i a doutance;	 do not apply iron to it, for there is doubt.
et se tu vois le malaide de fort vertut, et il n’a autre maladie que ydropisie soulement, et il n’est mie trop jones ne trop vielz, si dois ensi ovrer:	 and if you see the patient with strong strength, and they have no other disease except for edema alone, and they are not too old nor too young, then you should proceed as follows:
lieve le malaide droit sus tes mains, et li ministres presse le ventre em boutant l’aigue a la plus basse partie dou pis, puis pren le spatumile espinous selonc ceste forme:	 lay the patient flat on your hands, and the assistant presses the abdomen towards the lower part of the back, then take the pointed spatula as follows:
Et soit trenchans de II pars.	 And let it be cut through its second part.
a pointe, et toutevoie ne soit mie si entrans qu’il puist venir jusc’a l’intestine quant on le fiche ens, et ne le puist blecier;	 At the point, and it should not be so deep that it can reach the intestines when inserted, and it should not be burned.
puis regarde se li ydropisie est enjanree devers les intestines:	 Then look if the pus is directed towards the intestines:
si covient que tu fendes ensus de la boude III dois droit desoz sus lou poignil;	 you should make an incision below the abscess, three fingers' breadths right beneath the tip of the finger.
et se li ydropisie est por la maladie dou foie, si soit ta fendure au senestre de la boude III dois;	 and if the pus is due to liver disease, make your incision on the left side, three fingers' breadths.
et se c’est por la miuce, si soit a destre, et ne covient mie que li malaides gise sus la fendure que les superfluitez ne corrent a celui foible leu;	 and if it is due to the stone, make your incision on the right side, but do not let the patient lie over the incision so that the fluid does not flow to the weak side.
puis perce tout le cuir a l’estrument, et le boute, et lieve ta main a tout le spatumile entre le cuir et le syfac ausi com en escorchant a la quantiteit d’une ungle ou enqui entor;	 then pierce the skin with the instrument, push it in, and insert your hand into the hole up to the spatula, or as far as the thickness of a nail.
puis perce lou syfac tant que li spatumile viegne au leu vuit, et c’est li leus de l’aigue, puis le trai fuer, et i boute cest estrument de coi ci est li forme:	 Then pierce the shoulderblade until the spatula reaches its position, and it is the upper part [of the shoulder], then draw [it] out, and insert this instrument with the shape shown here:
Et est semblans a une caine d’argent subtil, et est d’arain ou d’archaut legier, et a en la partie desoz I petit pertus;	 And it resembles a thin silver chain and is made of iron or light lead, and at the lower part there are small holes.
et ou costeit d’une part, III pertus;	 And on one side, three small holes are placed.
et II d’autre part, et I d’autre;	 And two on the other side, and one on the other [side].
et est li chiés tailliez si com une penne, et c’est li forme de l’incision dont li escrivains taille la penne:	 And the head is shaped like a quill, and this is the shape of the incision that scribes make with their pen.
au chief desus est li alemele, si que quant li estrumens vient a l’aigue, si dessent maintenant sus l’estrument;	 On the top [of the head] is the handle, so that when the instrument comes to the upper part, press now on the tool.
vuide la donques la moitiet ou la tierce part, car se tu en vuides plus qu’il ne covient en celle houre, par aventure si muert li malaides por la resolution de son esperit de l’arme, ou il chiet paumez, ou il aproche a la mort;	 Empty then the half or the third part, for if you empty more than is necessary in that hour, accidentally, the patient might die due to the resolution of their spirit from the weapon, or they may fall down or approach death.
mais en vuide selonc la quantiteit de sa vertut, et selonc ceu que les dispositions de la vertut dou malaide signifient, et ses poulz;	 but empty according to its potency and according to what the patient's condition and pulse indicate.
puis trai l’estrument et retien l’aigue, et elle est retenue maintenant por le keur qui estoupe le pertus qui est sus le syfac, de coi j’ai parleit, que tu perces selonc ceste maniere;	 then draw the instrument and hold back the liquid, it is now retained for the caution that prevents bleeding from the wound, as I spoke about before, pierce in this manner.
puis rencomence l’estrument l’autre jor, se tu vois le malaide soffrant ceu, et trai de l’aigue une petite quantiteit;	 then use the instrument again on the next day if you see the patient suffering and draw a small amount of liquid.
fai ce aucun jor, et te garde de foloier tant qu’il ni demore mais c’un poc d’aigue.	 Do this every day, and avoid drinking too much water until it doesn't remain but a little.
Et se tu doutes sus le malaide, et tu i lais mout d’aigue, si le cure de la sepulture ou sablon chaut, et par mout sueir ou bain et au soleil, et se teigne de boivre;	 And if you doubt the patient, and give him too much water, cure it with the sepulchre or hot sand, and by sweating or bathing, and expose to the sun, and anoint with wine;
et le cure de medicines desiccatives tant qu’il soit sanez, et cauterize sus l’estomac et sus lou foie et sus l’esplen aprés l’estraction de l’aigue, si com j’ai dit devant.	 and cure it with drying medicines until it is healthy, and cauterize the stomach, liver, and spleen after the removal of water, as I have said before.
de l’estopement de la verge	Of the stopping of the penis
Aucune fois naissent enfant qui n’ont point de pertus en la verge, ou li pertus est petis, ou il n’est mie en son leu.	 Sometimes children are born who have no foreskin or whose foreskins are small and not in the right place.
Si le covient tantost qu’il n’aist percier a tout I spatumile molt subtil selonc ceste forme:	 If it is necessary that you make a very thin incision in all spittle-like places according to this form:
puis met ou pertus I clo subtil de plonc, et le lie et le tien ensi III jors ou IIII et quant il vuet faire urine, si soit ostez li clos, et faice urine, et puis li remet;	 Then place a small, thin cloth plug and hold it for 3 or 4 days until he wants to urinate, then remove the plug, let him urinate, and then replace it.
et par aventure nen i couvient point, car li urine qui vient fuer ne lou laisse close.	 And by chance it is not closed at all, because the urine that comes out does not keep it shut.
Cil de cui li pertus est petis, si est medicinez dou clo de plonc, si com nos avons dit, si s’eslargera.	 For the person whose wound is small, the treatment with a cup made of lead, as we have said, will expand.
Cil qui n’ont mie le pertus en lor leu sont bleciet, car aucun naissent qui ont le pertus au chief de la verge, por coi il ne puient pissier avant s’il ne lievent lor verge en haut;	 Those who do not have the foreskin in its place are circumcised, because no one is born with a foreskin on the head of the penis, which prevents them from urinating before they pull up their foreskin.
et ne pueent enjanrer por ceu que li matiere ne puet venir jusc’a la marris, et c’est une male maladie.	 and cannot copulate because the matter cannot reach the wife, and it is a bad disease.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos, puies estent le chief de la verge et le cope ausi com la taille d’une penne, si ke li pertus chiece em mileu, si com il covient;	 And the procedure is that the patient lies on his back, with the head of the penis and the tip placed as close together as the end of a feather, so that the foreskin meets in the middle, as it should.
et te garde de decorrement de sanc qui i vient maintes fois, et s’il avient, si l’estainche de ceu qui estainche sanc, et cure la plaie tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And beware of bleeding that often occurs, and if it happens, stop the bleeding from those who are bleeding, and heal the wound until it is healed.
des pustules de la verge	of the penis ulcers
Maintes fois vienent cist albathe en la verge, et est une apparance de char laide;	 Often this albatus appears in the penis, and it is a sign of bad flesh.
et en i a malignes et non malignes;	 And there are malignant and non-malignant ones in it.
si covient que tu les preignes a I oncine subtil, et les cope et munde toutes, puis met sus coton moilliet en oignement egiptien;	 You must grasp them with a very fine loop, strike and clean them all, then place dampened Egyptian cotton bandage on top.
puis le cure d’oignement diafinicon tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then cure it with diaphinicon ointment until it is healed.
Et se li albathe est maligne, de pute color et depuant, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere.	 And if the ulcer is malignant, of a greenish-yellow color and foul smelling, then you must apply cautery.
Quant tu l’as copeit, et se li albathe est en som la verge, et en ait partie dedens la peil et partie defuer, si covient que tu oste l’albathe qui est dedens premier;	 When you have struck it and the albathe is inside in the shaft and part within the skin and part outside, you must remove the inner albathe first.
et quant il est soudez, si le cure defuer.	 And when it is sutured, cure it externally.
Car quant tu le cures ensamble, si n’est mie asseurez li chiez de la verge qu’il ne soit perciez, et vient noiror et corruption en son la verge et ou coion;	 For when you cure it together, the shafts are not certain that they will not be pierced, and darkness and corruption come into the shaft and where it is.
si covient chever tout ceu qui est noir et corrumput, puis lie sus l’emplaustre de miel et de farine qui soit fait d’escorce de poumes grenates et de veces, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	 You must cover all that is black and corrupted, then bind it with an ointment made of honey and flour which is made from the peel of pomegranate rinds and vine leaves, then cure it with other remedies until it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si amenistre le cautere lunaire selonc ceste forme:	 And if there is discharge of blood, bring the lunar cautery as follows:
Li cauteres si aide as II dispositions ensamble:	 The cauteries aid in combined applications:
c’est asavoir, au decorrement de sanc, et a la corruption;	 it means, in the drawing of blood, and in rotting.
et se li chiés de la verge est corrumpus et retrais, si covient que tu boutes ou conduit de la verge une cainne de plonc, et pisse li malaides parmi;	 if the head of the penis is rotten and pulled out, it is necessary that you insert or lead a sheath of yew, and make the patient urinate.
et quant li pelz iert aerse au chief de la verge qui avient a ces qui n’ont mie esteit circoncis, ou il avient por plaie ou por aposteme, si covient donques que tu l’escorches a I estrument cheveit, tant que li liiens soit desliiez, et soit delivrez li chiez de la verge de toutes pars;	 if the skin is torn on the head of the penis, which happens to those who have not been circumcised, or it happens due to injury or abscess, then you must scrape it with the instrument of comb, until the ligaments are loosened, and the head of the penis is released from all sides.
et se c’est grief chose de deviser ceu, si covient que tu l’escorches a I spatumile aucun poc dou chief de la verge et de la peil;	 if it is necessary to talk about this, you must scrape it with the spatula slightly from the head of the penis and the skin.
puis dessevre belement entre II, et i met I subtil drapeil de lin moilliet an aigue froide, qu’il n’aerse derechief.	 Then gently insert it (the dislocated joint) between them (the two bones), and place a thin linen cloth dampened in cold water on it, so that it does not swell again.
de la circoncision	Of circumcision
Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies;	 Circumcision is not a continuous cutting as other wounds are;
toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.	 Nevertheless, when we perform this work of our own will and specifically on children, it is necessary that we do the best and easiest work for their salvation.
Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.	I say that the ancients did not circumcise their children, for it is not in their law, and we have only what we have acquired through experience.
Car j’ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor I dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule;	 Because I have seen the majority of masters and healers who perform circumcisions around there (the area), using force, and without using anesthesia.
si fuioit li keurs car il i a II toiles, et par aventure si cope on celi desus et demore celle desoz.	 the pain is avoided because there are two cloths (or layers), and by chance if one of them is struck above, the one below remains.
Or la recovient coper, et est li dolor double, et a la mundification qui est dou dal n’est mie asseuree li pointe dou membre;	 And it (should) recover covered, and the pain is doubled, and at the cleansing which is deep in the limb, there is no assurance of the point of the member.
et a la mundification de l’ungle par aventure eschaipe li fer, et corront l’uevre, et maintes fois naissent ensi qu’il n’ont mestier de mundification et je l’ai veut.	 And in the cleaning of the nail by chance, the iron may slip, and it will spoil the work, and many times (it) arises so that there is no need for cleansing, and I have seen this happen.
De la mondification qui est faite as forces a tout le liien de fil ai je troveit la bonteit de l’experiment, car les forces taillent justement ausi bien desus com desoz.	In the amputation which is made all through the thread of iron I have found the benefit of the experiment, for the saw cuts exactly as well above as below.
Car quant tu presses ta main, si tailles igalment en I tout soul tens;	 For when you press your hand, cut evenly all the time;
mais que li filz soit bien estrois entor lou cuir;	 but that the thread be well tightened around the skin.
et soit li maniere dou premier ovraige si est que tu faices penser l’enfant, s’il entent, que tu ne li fais fuer que liier le fil entor la verge tant soulement, et pues le fai esjoir en toutes les manieres que tu pues;	 and the manner of the first work is that you make the child understand that you only bind the thread around the penis, and then let it be relieved in all ways that you can.
puis le fai ester entre tes mains tout droit, et repont les forces entre tes mains ou desoz tes piez que li enfes ne les voie, ne aucun des estrumens;	 Then make it be between your hands straight, and press the forces between your hands or under your feet so that the infant does not see them, nor any of the tools.
puis boute ta main a la verge et souffle ou keur, et la trai en haut tant que li chiés de la verge soit ens;	 Then place your hand at the neck and blow or squeeze, and draw it up as far as the head of the neck is in.
puis la mundifie bien de l’ordure qui i est assemblee, puis lie le leu signiet d’un fil double, puis la lie desoz I poc a I autre liien;	 then clean it well of the filth that has gathered there, then tie the joint with a double thread, then tie it under the foot to another cord.
et la tien as II dois par la seconde lieeure au pouchet et au doit indice, et cope entre les II liiens, puis lieve le keur desus hastanment et trai le chief de la verge;	 and hold it as required by the second knot at the elbow and the wrist, and press between the two cords, then pull the cord quickly upwards and draw the head of the neck.
puis laisse corre le sanc poc et poc, car c’est li muedres;	 Then let the blood come out little by little, for it is the healing process.
et met poudre sus et sus la poudre I drapeil glueit d’un moieuf d’uef cuit destempreit d’aigue rose, confit avec oile roset boin et fres, et lou laisse sus jusc’a l’autre jor, et le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And pour powder on top and above the powder, you stick a glue made from cooked egg white steeped in rose water, mixed with fresh and good rose oil, and leave it on until the next day, and treat it with another treatment until it is healed.
Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste:	 The shape of the force during the healing process is as follows:
li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	 The two shoulders should be tender and sharp, and the shoulders equally as wide as the hand.
li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision;	 The error in healing is when the cavity within is incised.
donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme;	 Therefore you must stretch it with your nail so that it becomes an abscess.
et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.	 And stretch it equally, and if you cannot hold it with your nail, then take tweezers and stretch it.
Et s’il trespassent III jors, et ceu qui est desoz la verge est enflez, si le laisse tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et l’escorche legierement;	 And if they exceed three days, and what is beneath the scrotum swells, let it be until the abscesses have subsided, and lightly incise (or lance) the skin.
si le cope si com tu pues mues, et te garde de la partie de la verge, ce ne li nuira niant.	 If the head can move like you can move it, and keep away from the area of the scrotum, it will not be harmed.
Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s’on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point;	 Then treat the wound with healing powders, as we have said or treated with powders, and if it moves too much, it will go above (or grow), but it will not be harmed.
cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then treat it (the wound) until it heals.
dou retenement de l’urine	Retention of urine
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division;	 The retention of urine is due to a stone in the bladder, or frozen blood, or watery stool, or a child born dead, or similar things, as we have said in the division (section).
et se li urine n’est desliie , et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz;	 And if the urine is not released, and you see it is retained due to a stone or neck of the bladder, then the patient should be bent over his knees;
et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet;	 and the feet should be placed on the back, extend his belly from above the lower back, and restrain the patient as much as he can;
et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e;	 then the neck of the bladder is pressed towards the expression of the stone above it, so that the urine is released;
et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme:	 and if it does not come as we have said, and the patient feels great pain, then you must provide extraction with all the instruments called "syringe," of which this is its form:
et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil;	 And let it be of fine silver thread, as thin as a bird's feather;
et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	 And let the cable be a palm and a half long, and be fine at one end.
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren I fil double, et lie au chief I poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue;	 And the manner of the urine outflow is that you take a double thread, tie one end of the cotton or woolen yarn to it and push the threaded end into the syringe;
et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus I siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede;	 and squeeze the excess of the cotton and push it up to the top of the syringe, then anoint the syringe with oil or butter and egg yolk, and make the patient sit on a chair, and rub the bladder and penis with moist oil and olive oil and cold water;
puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude;	 Then gently insert the syringe into the rod, until it reaches the root of the rod, then bend the rod above towards the buttock.
puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors;	 Then place the syringe towards the bladder, and make the patient feel it arrive at the empty spot, and this is not done according to this order for any other reason than because the one guiding it makes a turn.
puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine;	 Then wind the thread around all the woolen yarn, and make the patient urinate following the yarn, then remove it, and correct the urine.
et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	 Then repeat the syringe until the bladder is empty and the patient is relieved.
des maladies de la vessie	On the diseases of the bladder
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	When scorches or blood comes in the bladder, or pus is assembled there and you see it distill liquids and medicines, then use all the instruments called "clepsydra", and this is its form:
Elle est close, et si a III pertus:	 It is closed, and if it has been pierced three times:
II d’une part, et I d’autre, si com tu vois;	 One on one side, and the other on the other; as you see.
et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est;	 And the joints of the neck shall be closed in such a way that the medicine is thick enough to stop the worm, if one can drain the moisture and insert what is necessary;
et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens;	 And when you see that you throw your medicine into the bladder, put the head of the cuestour in the moisture and draw out the worm that is there;
si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens;	 If you draw out the moisture from the cuestour, then push the drawing hard;
si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira;	 The worm will enter into it (the cuestour), and will come to the bladder now, so that the patient will feel it.
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie:	 And this is the form of the subtle enema with which one instills the bladder:
si est ci:	 If it is here (meaning the patient):
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut;	 And it is of silver or iron, and the head is raised higher;
et desoz a I sein ou li liiens chiet;	 and under the arm where the bones fall;
puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les II seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe I poc celle moistor sus le feu;	 then take a sheep bladder and put the moisture which you use to cleanse the bladder, then tie it between the two breasts with good doubled thread, and heat that moisture over the fire;
puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie;	 then insert the head of the bladder into the penis, then hold your hand on the bladder with all the moisture coming out, until the patient feels that the moisture has reached the bladder;
et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai I cercle, et le perce rondement entor;	 and if you do not have a bladder, take a piece of parchment, make a circle, and pierce it roundly;
puis boute I fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble I dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument;	 Then push the strong thread into those wounds, then gather the circle in the same way one gathers a thimble, and put oil, moisture, and water inside it and tie it in the instrument.
et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	 And do as you have done with the bladder, pressing with your hand until the moisture comes to the bladder.
de la piere	From the stone
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines;	 We have already said in the section on stones about the methods of extraction and medicines.
et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille;	 I have also said the difference between a stone embedded in the flesh and all the signs, and for which stones one should operate with incision.
et en la vessie, et en la verge;	 and in the bladder, and in the penis;
et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	 And I will tell you clearly and briefly.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit;	 I say that the stone embedded in the bladder occurs more often in children, and it is a sign that water jumps out of the bladder like water in its subtlety.
et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist;	 And he opens an hernia, and greatly stretches the patient's vein, and pierces it many times, then ties it.
et a mout de ces saut li fondemens;	 And for these reasons, the foundations are filled with fear.
et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont IIII ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece;	 And children's healing is light until they are four years old, and it is very serious in the elderly, and it is moderate in those who are between youth and old age.
et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	 And the treatment of large arrows is lighter than that of small ones.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines.	 And when we come to treatment, it is first necessary to purify the patient with an enema, in order to draw out all the feces that are in the intestines.
Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	 For it sometimes obstructs seeking the stone.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut;	 Then take the patient by the feet, and bend them back and move downwards so that the arrow points to the depth of the bladder, and withdraw it once towards the top.
puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval;	 Then make him sit between your hands prepared, and his hands should be below his thighs, so that the bladder is completely descending downwards.
puis la quier et la touche dedens;	 Touch it inside and hold it there.
se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.	 If you feel the stone in the space, hasten now to cut into the stone.
Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis;	 And if it does not fall at the touch, moisten your left index finger with oil, if the patient is an infant, or use your thumb, if the patient is a fully-grown young person.
et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie;	 Push it into its foundation, press the stone, and when you feel it with your finger, pull the stone to the neck of the bladder.
puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	 Then press on it with your finger and push it towards the place where you intend to cut.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille;	 And command the assistant to press the bladder with his hand, and command him to spread his right hand upwards, and with his left hand peel off the skin that is under the testicles in the area where the cutting is to be done.
puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	 Then push the large spatula, of which it is the shape:
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre;	 And place it between that which is between the cheeks and the bottom, not in the middle but at the left side of the nose.
et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans;	 and be straight above the stone, and your thumb should be at the bottom or base, and the tip of the spatula should be wide in length but narrow within, according to the size of the stone, not too large.
par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail;	 In case the pressure on the thumb which is at the base causes it to jump out due to effort.
et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges:	 And know that there are several stones or areas with edges and borders:
si est griés a issir;	 if it is gritted out (? - not sure about this one);
et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	 And if there is a concave area, similar to a plum pit and rounded, from which the stone easily emerges.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant;	 For the one with angles and edges, make the cut larger.
et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe;	 And if it does not jump, then you must press with pliers that are similar to a chisel at the tip, to forcibly move the stone so that it does not escape.
ou tu boute desoz li I estrument subtil corbé au chief;	 or you push underneath the instrument curved slightly at the tip.
et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge I poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole;	 and if you cannot maneuver it in this way, then enlarge the small opening a bit, and if it does not burst out, stretch it with glass.
et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors.	 and if there are more than one stone, then push the largest one against the bladder's neck first, then strike it, then pull it, and the smaller ones afterwards if there are more.
Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie.	 If it is very large, it must be made larger by making a bigger incision.
Car II choses avienent au malaide:	 For two things happen to the sick person:
ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder;	 or he dies, or the urine comes immediately due to the loins which cannot be sealed.
mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces;	 but still make efforts to drain it, or break it with pincers, as you draw it in pieces.
et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus I drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut;	 and when you have completed your work, apply the wound with incense and aloe and dragon's blood, bind it, and put on it a damp cloth soaked in oil and vinegar, or in oil and cold rose water and cold water, to cool the abscess.
puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	 then lay the sick person on his neck and do not undo the ligature until the third day.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you undo it (the bindings), immerse the wound well in oil and water, then apply the ointment "dyafinicon" and "basilicon" until it is healed.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine:	 And if an abscess swells and corrodes in the wound, or freezing of blood occurs in the bladder, and as a result the urine is retained, which is known to come without jumping with the urine:
boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit;	 Therefore draw your knife on the wound, and extract that blood, for if it remains there, the bladder will burst, and it will be ruined.
puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 Lift the wound of pus and pus-like matter, and help it in every way you know, until it is healed.
et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les II cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	 And it is necessary that all the wounds you treat, that you tie them together with bandages, and apply the medicine on top of the wound.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir;	 If the stone is small and it is led from the urethra and thrust in, and the urine cannot come out;
si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure.	 if you treat this as I have said, that you cut it many times, then you are excused from punishment for this treatment.
Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	 I have already experienced this.
Pren .i. foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a .iij. angles fichiees en .i. tison:	Take one iron rod in the shape as follows and sharpened at four angles, pointed on one thread:
puis pren I fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie;	 Then take the thread and tie it around the rod beneath the stone, so that it cannot return to the bladder.
puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere;	 Push the drill lightly into the rod until it reaches the stone.
et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part;	 Turn the drill gently in the stone, bit by bit, as you can pierce the stone from the other side.
si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge.	 The urine will soon come out, then press your hand on what remains of the stone inside the rod.
Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides;	 It will be broken and fly out with the urine, and the patient is cured.
et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie I fil desoz la piere et I autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les II liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie;	 If you cannot do this for any reason that prevents it, tie the thread around the stone and the other end outside, then push the rod towards the stone between the two threads, pull it out, and untie the thread, and clean the frozen blood from the wound.
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And heal until he is sound.
de la piere des femmes	from women's stones (kidney stones)
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por III choses:	 It happens that stone be engendered in women, and if it ever occurs, the cure is difficult, and it is forbidden for three reasons:
l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge;	 The first is that perhaps the woman is a virgin;
et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	 And the second one is that it cannot be found a woman well versed who undresses herself in front of mirrors, especially when she is chaste.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains;	 And the third one is that by chance it cannot be found a woman well versed in this handcraft.
et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a. Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier I caste mire subtil;	 And the fourth way is that the stone of a woman is deeper than that of a man, for this reason you must make a more profound incision and it causes great fear. And if you need to do it, then you must take a skilled midwife, and even though she is hard to find, do not resort to using an unchaste mirror;
et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere;	 and show a wise bailiff in the affairs of women or a woman who knows some part of the art, and command her to do what you command in the incision of the stone.
et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge:	 And examine very well if the woman is a virgin:
adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere;	 Then one must place the finger or probe and search for the stone.
et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	 and if it is found, one should hold it with the finger under it, and instruct the woman to push her hand or press against the patient, and search and press her left hand on the bladder.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse;	 If it is found, it should be moved gently from the entrance of the bladder downwards until it reaches the root of the thigh.
puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie;	 Then strike the stone at the root of the thigh near the mons pubis, where it can be moved easily, and feel the stone in that area.
et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite;	 and do not move the finger above or below the stone, and cut it (the stone) at first small parts;
puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont:	 Then push the iron into the abdomen, if you feel the arrow, press the wound so that the arrow can come out easily, and know that there are many kinds of arrows.
c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains.	 this is to know: small and large, sharp and smooth, long and round, and those with grooves.
si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	 know the appearances to understand the outcome.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	 And if the arrow escapes you, put it in its place with broken vitriol and hold it for an hour until the wound is cauterized.
puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre;	 Then return to your work until the arrow is out, and have tools that I told you about in extracting the arrow for men to help you in your task.
et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide;	 and if the arrow escapes you, and it is an artery that is cut, put powder on the place and hold with tourniquets and bandages, do not start again, let the arrow be and do not draw it out, for there is danger the patient may die.
puis cure la plaie.	 Then treat the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the heat of the blood has subsided and the wounds have closed, return to your work, until the arrow is expelled.
de hernie carnouse	of a carnous hernia
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef;	 Aquous (is) nothing other than a collection of moisture or white chalk which is beneath the coil of the egg, containing water.
et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit I autre oef;	 and is called "syfac," and sometimes it is properly in the eggshell, if one thinks that it is another egg.
et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit;	 and it is the membrane of the shell between the white chalk (we have said).
et ceu n’avient se poc non.	 It does not happen unless there is a hole (in the shell).
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the growth of this hernia is due to weakness that comes from the bladder, and the matter spreads out.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors:	 And sometimes it comes from impact on the eggshell, and this moisture has many colors:
ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus;	 or it is yellowish discoloration, or without redness, or black, or white watery liquid, and this happens more often.
et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, I poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	 And these are the signs to recognize this assembly, for if it is white and shapeless as we have said, it is an abscess; it is long like an egg, and does not open the eyes, for it has moisture all around.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef;	 And if there is moisture in the very cloth (of the abscess), it is an abscess with a part of an egg and for that reason one thinks that it is another egg.
et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien;	 And if there is moisture between the outer layer (of the eye) and the white shapeless (area), one can feel it well.
donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	 Therefore, when you wish to know the color of the moisture, you must test with all the introducer (instrument) and thus determine its form as mentioned above.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	Accordingly, judge what is inside based on the probe that comes afterwards.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors;	 And when we treat it with iron, the patient should be purified to our ability and the filling of his body.
puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz;	 Then lay him on his back, upon something slightly high, and put much cloth under him.
puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des II costelz dou keur des coions;	 then lie him on his left side, and instruct the assistant to sit on the right, and extend the rod to one of the two ribs near the shoulders.
puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir;	 then take the spatula, strike the skin of the shoulders along its length down to the end of the tip, and make the incision straight in dividing the skin of the shoulders up to the elbow, and peel it off delicately according to your ability.
puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a I large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont;	 then pierce the skin deeply with water, and draw out all the water, and then put your fingers, and stretch the skin upward.
et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement;	 And do not touch the heart of the kidneys, but only the bladder.
cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue;	 Cut through or in pieces the ribcage of him finely, otherwise if you do not cut it skillfully, the wound will return.
et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac;	 If the egg jumps in your work, reset it in its place when you have completed the work with the bladder.
puis assemble les II leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then assemble the two bellies of the kidneys in one stitch, then heal it as with other wounds, until it is healed.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc;	 And if you find the egg corrupted by another disease, it is necessary that you tie the vessels that are suspended, fearing the discharge of blood.
puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	 Then cut the kidney with everything attached and extract the egg, and heal it as we have said.
Et se aigue est assemblee en II parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont II ramices;	 And if the humerus is assembled in two parts together, know that these are two branches;
si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset;	 If the other part is placed similarly to how you did the first one, then squeeze out the blood and put moistened linen soaked in rose oil on the wound.
et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les II coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	 and put another piece of moistened linen soaked in wine and oil on both sides, and place bandages over them, and tie it all up with the same kind of string as shown here.
Puis pren II drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil;	 Then take the bandages and fill them with hempen cloth as shown here, sewn together in the shape of a collar for the arm, one end grasps the base up to the back, the other at the handle.
et li autre dui chief sus les II angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier;	 And the other shoulder joint is placed on top of the two angles, and all the rest is gathered in the bracelet loop.
et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes I cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers;	 At times, this ramie (or bandage) of fire cautery is used in place of iron size, and it is that you take the cauterizing cultellar knife, touch the skin of the wound, and let it be heated as we have said, so that the whitish substance containing the aqueous fluid is exposed;
si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	 if you take the cautery in this form and pierce the whitish substance at once with it, then scrape off that thin layer of heated cautery;
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout;	 And beat it in all ways as you can until it is burned completely.
et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef;	 and make sure the fire does not touch the egg (meaning: yolk).
et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve;	 And know that this work is more wholesome;
et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille;	 and moves guarding against bleeding, and moistens that the works of cutting;
et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	 and if nothing happens contrary to you, or abscesses swell or bleeding or something else, treat what happens contrary to you, according to what has been said before;
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai, si fai seoir le malaide sus I siege leveit;	 And if the patient is afraid and does not wish to wait for this work because of its horror, introduce perforation as I tell you, and it is that when you are quite certain through the signs we have said that a hernia is present, make the patient sit on an elevated seat;
pues perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors;	 then pierce the abscess in the part beneath all the spoutulum wide and place the perforation along the length of the body.
et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer;	 And let the wounds be wide, so that all the sharp corners flow freely;
puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee;	 then place cotton on the wound, tie it up, and let the remaining blood flow freely, then cure it until the wound is healed;
et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant;	 and if the white cloth does not allow blood to flow from the wound's mouth, then you must put a feather or instrument for draining fluid from hydropics into it, as described previously;
et eslarge I poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés VI mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.	 and widen the wound, check that the blood returns, and wait for it to heal, which is about 6 months or more, and when it heals as described before, the patient will recover their health.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the abscess of the kidneys
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse;	 Check that in the section of this artery there is fear of various positions, so it seems to me that it is better to leave it.
et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	 And I shall tell you the work and the likeness of an abscess.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions;	 Then many abscesses come in bodies, and especially in joints;
et c’est par mout de cas.	 And this happens frequently.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion;	 This is caused by an excess of sour and wet, which is spread in the kidneys or by trauma.
et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors;	 The color of the abscess follows the body's complexion;
et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief;	 No pain is found, and the abscess is severe.
et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	 Sometimes an abscess is hard and stony, of such color, and at times comes from the artery or swelling of a vein.
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois;	 When it is due to an artery, it can be recognized by the hot swelling of the abscess when you press with your fingers.
et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	 It should not be touched.
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois, et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars;	 An abscess caused by swelling of a vein can be recognized by its appearance when touched with the fingers and can be safely cut open in this case and in similar cases.
et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	 And it is that you cut the core of the cheeks, then lift up the egg, and pull the thread from the white yolk, and free the suspension of all parts of the egg.
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope;	 If the egg is already softened with these born charms, then it is necessary that you draw the egg and crush it.
et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	 And if it is swollen in the yolk, or in that which is within the vessels, you must release all that softness, and crush it thoroughly.
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	And if the birth of the hernia is at the rear end, you should cut it all out and extract the egg as we have said.
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	When your work is done, apply the wound with moistened linen in rose oil and wine, then heal it with other treatments until it heals.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the abscess of the kidneys
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a I borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions, et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait;	 This is an abscess wrapped in a covering resembling a purse, with the softening of the cheeks, and the patient becomes silent as he goes.
et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant, et toutevoie nos vos dirons l’ovraige de li, selonc ceu que li ancien firent.	 And the cure for this disease is as risky as the one before, and yet we will tell you its work, according to what the ancients did.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege aleveit, puis li boute le suspensoire des coions aval a tes dois, a tout le vasseil qui sont prochien a la verge, et les teigne li maistres, et les estende forment;	 You must make the patient sit on an elevated seat, then push the suspension ligament from the coccyx down towards your hands, to all the vessels that are near the verge, and mark them with the master's fingers, and stretch them out fully.
puis cope au spatumile trenchant large dou traver endroit les vasselz, tant qu’il soient descovert, et puis escorche de chescune part, si com nos avons dit en l’estraction des arteres qui sont en temples;	 Then with a sharp pointed spatula, wide enough to reach the vessels, uncover them and then skin from both sides, as we have said in the extraction of the arteries that are in the temples.
puis i fiche une aguille ou il ait I fil double, et le lie au premier leu ou li vis est venue, et le lie derechief a l’autre chief;	 Then insert a needle with double thread and tie it to the first place where blood has appeared, and then tie it to the other side.
puis les cope em mileu droitement, selonc la longesce dou cors, et en trai les moistors corrumpues;	 Then strike it in the middle directly, according to the length of the body, and pull out the corrupt moisture.
puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions;	 Then heal the wound as one would heal another [similar] wound, so that no animal cheeps that is fed by either side [of the wound].
car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz;	 for in this way no harm comes, and if all the animals come to it, then you must draw blood from all of them.
si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	 so that the eyes do not lose their milk due to the wounds of animals, and they dry up and cannot help themselves.
de la routure dou syfac	From the rupture of the sifac
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions;	 The consequences of this dislocation are by the section that comes out or the extension above the stomach in the area of the inguinal region, which is why the intestines descend from that cut through one of the eyes.
et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces II manieres de mout de causes:	 and this cut is either the syphac or the extension of it, and these two types of wounds come from many causes:
ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses;	 or of percussion, or of a jump, or of a fall, or of lifting a heavy load, and similar things;
et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement;	 and the signs when it is of stretching the sinew, are that it happens little by little, over a long time, and does not come suddenly.
et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	 and abscesses are equal towards the full, because the sinew follows the intestines.
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	And the signs when it is of the section of the dislocation, are that it brings sudden pain at the beginning, and the abscesses appear differently, under the skin near, and this is due to the outflow of the intestine and the body turning away from the dislocation.
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	And sometimes the intestines come out through the hernia, and are retained there, and cause great pain to suffer for the patient, especially when it is pressed.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	And in these iron treatments there is fear, therefore it is necessary to escape from them.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir;	 And the method of work is that you instruct the patient to pull the intestine with their hand into the wound if they can reach it.
puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes;	 then put it on its neck. hold it between your hands, and lift the legs;
puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc;	 then stretch the skin above, and cut all the hide of the cheeks with long strokes;
puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir;	 Then insert the little fingers of the waist deeply according to what is necessary to open the wound, and so that the thumb can come out.
puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars;	 Then peel off the flesh that is beneath the skin of the nails, until the white flesh under the skin is exposed all around.
puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac;	 Then insert your index finger into the nail where the nail and the white flesh under the skin meet, between the second layer of flesh, and separate the part that is behind the fingernail and between the second layer of flesh.
et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille;	 And then move your right hand inside the nail cavity, and lift the white flesh upward to your left hand, and peel off the fingernail entirely in the direction of the waist.
et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement;	 And command the minister to extend the arm upwards, and untie the one that is behind the elbow.
et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz;	 And if there is any evidence of the intestines wrapped around or hardened white matter, and if you find anything like that, push it into the abdomen.
puis pren une aguille ou il ait I gros fil fait de X filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions;	 Then take a needle with a thick thread made from X threads, and push it into the back part of the white matter, which is after the hide of the kidneys.
