aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait IIII filz;	 After the waist, then cut the hairs that appear from the threads, as long as there are four threads.
puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de II pars;	 Then put them one on top of the other in a cross shape and tie the white matter, as we have said is behind the hide of the kidneys, with a strong knot of 2 parts.
puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de II pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne;	 Then wrap the heads of the fingers, and tie them together with two bands, so that no one feeding them can enter into it, except abscess pus comes in.
et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc II dois de celui, et aprés ces II liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi;	 and place the linen straight according to the first linen of that length two times its own, and afterwards leave a small opening at the end where the swelling is near the bones a finger's width.
et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte;	 And after all the rest according to the roundness that the egg bears;
puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant;	 Then cut in the part that is beneath the skin of the eyes, as much as it requires without damaging it, and bend, as we have said before.
puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	 Then bring dampened wool in oil, apply it to the wounds, and bring the thread that we have mentioned.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	And sometimes the whites are cauterized as we have said, after the incision, due to fear of bleeding.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui;	 For this often happens, and let the thread stay until it has closed up.
et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece;	 And if it takes a long time to close, warm it with hot water and apply what we have said on it until it has closed.
puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	 Then treat the wound with another remedy, until it is perfectly healed.
de hernie carnouse	of a carnous hernia
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this case, I never saw anyone who dared to perform the cure with iron.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;	 And the ancients said that it is made like a sprig of willow, in this manner you tie the branches after cutting them lightly below.
puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient;	 Then cut it [the affected area] in half, and treat the abscess of those who work [the area], until the pus stops.
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And heal as we have said, until it is healthy.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus;	 Sometimes gangrene comes in wounds, as we have said, and open the limbs.
et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres;	 And do not remove any of the internal organs such as bowels, and if some are removed, it is bad, and repair them every hour.
et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent;	 Furthermore, if it remains too long in this place, the wound or fester, as long as the internal organs are being removed.
et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert;	 This happens due to the spread of the fester which is in wounds, as we have said, because it is extended, then the limbs are softened and inflamed and opened.
et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit;	 And the cure is by cautery, as we have previously said;
et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere:	 Sometimes it is healed by iron in this manner:
et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de III dois;	 and the patient lies supine on his back between your hands, then strike the swelling at the wound site according to the size of three fingers;
et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac;	 and draw out the pus that is under the skin, then take the iron and place it on the visible part of the abscess;
et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les II leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre;	 and press down deeply into the belly, then burn the two visible parts of the abscess on top of the iron tip, one after the other;
puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines;	 then remove the iron tip, and do not cover or extend the abscess or anything else, as I have previously told you in the treatment of the ramie of the intestines;
puis le cure par la cure des plaies.	 Then treat it with wound treatment.
Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	 And when you cut the threads (sutures), if it becomes infected and heals the wound, let it remain until it is healed.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	The fistula (li sifac) is closed, and it has no appearance in the wound, and the cauterization is performed in this place, and it is closer to salvation.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	of the softening of the skin around the eyes
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir;	 Often, the skin around the eyes becomes soft in some men due to the internal charms being softened and there is pus visible.
et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil;	 It is necessary, when one wants to treat it, that you make the patient lie down on their back, and strike the softened skin on the natural skin.
puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a III costures ou IIII fermement;	 Then bring the two lips together in a stitch, and if you see, first make a seam for the excess skin softened with three or four stitches firmly.
puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	 Then strike between the stitches, and the wound as with other wounds, until it is healed, and cut the thread.
dou chastrement	The punishment or correction (of a patient)
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre;	 Know that amputations are condemned in our law, and for this reason I would not like to speak about them in this book.
et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres:	 And it is not necessary unless for two reasons:
dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure;	 because the mirror in amputation answers when asked, and in amputation, the treatment.
et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	 And the other, because we often need to use training with some animals to help us, such as goats and sheep and cats and others.
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres:	 Then I say that trainings are done in two ways:
ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	 or by attraction, or by cutting.
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant;	 In that which we do by attraction, let us sit the beast in hot water until its joints are softened and loosened.
puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	 Hold them with your hand until they are set and you no longer feel them.
Du chastrement de taille:	 The cautery of the incision:
covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez;	 It is necessary that you mark the beast, and press the skin of the hocks with your left hand, then tie the thong, and strike on each ear when you have well flayed them;
et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz;	 and leave any small piece of flesh or subtle flesh that is on the hooves;
et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure;	 And this method of cauterization is better than the one made by attraction, because at attraction something from the hocks may remain accidentally, causing the beast to desire lust;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	 Then heal the wound until it is healed.
des hermofrodites	Hermaphrodites (intersex individuals)
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes:	 Hermaphroditus is according to two kinds of humans:
l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	 One such case is when there are two openings wide apart as in the shape of a woman's figure with hair between them and sometimes urinating inside (courting).
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	 And the other method is in women, and it has above the hilt like a rod and they pierce it.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies;	 And the treatment for the man and the woman is that you press the closed wounds together and treat them as other wounds;
en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	 In the second manner, in men whose urine jumps through the skin of the scrotum, there is no cure.
de la tentigene	The translation for this line is:
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir;	 Tumor is a closed wound on the natural part, as long as it is too unsightly to see;
et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	 And some women have them as large as a hand, and this is the treatment.
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement;	 You must dye the excess of the tumor with your hand or any cloth and press it gently;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	 And do not go too deep, so as not for blood to flow out, then cure it with other cure until it is healed.
et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	 And to another sore that arises at the mouth of the womb, and the membrane bursts, and by chance it jumps out, and it resembles a cow's disease, and for this reason it is called the "cow disease" by the ancients.
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	 It must be cut as we have said before, and it should be cured until it is healed.
de erratique	From erratic [or wandering]
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis;	 It is erratic when the nature of a woman is not perceived or if the wound is small.
et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est;	 And it may be by natural birth or accident due to disease that comes upon it.
ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit;	 Or it may be a sore joined together, or from the subtle matter of pus, and is made deep in the womb, or in the flanks, or inside, or anywhere else.
et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir;	 Prevent conception, pregnancy, and flowers to grow.
et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	 And the knowledge of these things is through the observation of the belly.
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	 If the discharge approaches, it may be in your hand or at your side.
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi:	 If it is a soft and subtle pain near the liver, hurry and search for it in this manner:
met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes;	 Place your two index fingers together, and the woman lies on her back, spreading her legs.
puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens;	 Then feel the two livers form, until the soft subtle pain is found, and be aware of the openings.
puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	 Then take linen, dampen it in oil, and place it on the place, let the woman lie flat each day, so that it cannot adhere.
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	 And if the wound is hard and thick, you should cut it with a spatula resembling a myrtle leaf.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope;	 If the opening is of new cheese, suspend it to an onion and cover it with clay.
et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef;	 And have the medicine to stop blood, such as alum, dragon's blood, incense, and egg yolk in abundance.
puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder;	 then introduce a broad strip of linen cloth so that the wound cannot be sutured.
et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec;	 and it should remain long, and you should also provide a dry tent made of linen.
puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then let it be healed by other treatments until it is healed.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	 And when a child is born in marriage, it should be covered according to this manner, unless abscesses are swollen.
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	 To the swollen abscess that is within marriage, one should not make any attempt to touch it.
des emorroides	Hemorrhoids [or Piles]
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul;	 Hemorrhoids are openings of veins without cortical treatment, and when hemorrhoids become old, they become hard.
et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	 And as we said in the division, their likenesses and signs, and I will say here those that receive treatment.
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	 I say that hemorrhoids and piles, when they are fully formed in marriage, and cannot be felt, are not cured by iron.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	 Those at the mouth of the sore, which can be felt, are those who can be healed.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses;	 Therefore you must put the woman in a cold house, then boil the eel to the point of tenderness, and chop it into its roots, then sprinkle powdered medicine that stops blood, such as alum and dragon's blood and incense, and similar things.
puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide;	 Then place his feet on the surface for an hour, then put them in cold water.
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	 If bleeding occurs, make it sit in a decoction of sumac bark, apple peel, hawthorn and similar things, then take barley flour, mix it with honey and egg yolk, and apply it as a plaster on its back.
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	 And if it stops bleeding, it is good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir;	 If not, make him wear armpits on his back and avoid hitting the breasts;
puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	 Then take linen, wet it in juices of plantain or marsh-mallow with old wine, and apply it to the place.
Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	 And when the abscess rests, treat the place with ointment until it is healed;
et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul;	 And the one called "albathir" is red, and resembles a sharp head. It needs to be covered as I mentioned in the remedy.
et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then nurse it until it is healed.
des apostemes de la marris	emorroidal openings (of the anus)
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	 Many types of abscess come in marriage, such as boils and hard abscesses, herpes, scabs, fissures, hemorrhoids, hot abscesses, and many other diseases that I mentioned in the classification.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe;	 Therefore, I must explain in this treatise the hot abscess that comes in marriage, which is not like other abscesses.
et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	 And if you wish to know the work of iron, look to see if the abscess is acute at the beginning of its arrival, and full of heat and fever, and becomes red if you can see it.
Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie;	 Then do not hasten to pierce [the abscess], but allow it to mature until the pain is eased;
et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus I siege, et ait II petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe;	 Then make the patient sit on a low stool or he may lean, and support his back and gather his feet at the parts away from the leg.
et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien;	 Spread his thighs, place his arms under his knees, and bind them well with a good linen.
puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme;	 Then suck the boil towards the right side, and introduce the instrument with which one operates the mouth of the bladder, by which follows the shape.
et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide;	 It is necessary that when you introduce this instrument, that you pierce the right side first to know the depth of the bladder, so that what enters within from the instrument does not go deeper than it should, and does not prick the patient.
et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve;	 And if the incision is larger, it is necessary to cover the depth of the wound with cloth, so that the incision does not hurt.
et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument.	 And it is necessary to put the handle of the instrument on top and to heat the instrument.
Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit;	 And when the abscess opens, and one touches it with a soft hand, it must be covered with a linen cloth.
et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec;	 And when the boil is empty, you must put damp and oiled rags or dry green oil in the wound.
et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites;	 And put a clean and damp linen cloth inside the wound, and on the outside of the wound and on the handle of the instrument place a hot or mustard-soaked linen cloth.
puis le cure aprés II jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 Then the patient is cured after two days of ointment application, as long as he is healthy.
et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites;	 And sometimes they lift the sore and the wound by cleansing with water and honey, and then with water or liquorice roots and long-cooked Aristolochia.
puis reveigne a l’oignement.	 Then return to the ointment application.
Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	 And if the wound is sutured in the flesh, you should avoid iron cautery, but treat it as we have said in the section.
de l’enfantement	From childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar:	 Firstly, the woman should know the form of natural childbirth, and the signs when you see the woman after pressing from below, and desire to urinate.
adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir;	 Then, the child hastens to be born with force.
adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui;	 Therefore, recognize that the childbirth is according to the natural form, and it comes out with its head, and the afterbirth follows.
et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost;	 And when you see these signs, it is necessary to gently press his stomach, so that the child comes out quickly.
car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification;	 for when he descends upon his head, the second one follows with him, and the husband of his superfluidities is cleansed by good purification.
et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.	 and this one who comes in another way does not come naturally.
Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises;	 For sometimes he comes upon his feet, and the belly or shoulder, or hands, or upon the stomach or spine, and is transformed accidentally at the neck, and in other bad shapes.
si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	 it is necessary that the bailiff be wise and skilled in these matters, and guard against error and deception, and I will show you all the shapes in which one should help them.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent;	 If a child comes upon the head by natural birth, and the woman gives birth with difficulty, and the strength of the child is weak, make her sit on a saddle, or have women hold her.
et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	 and anoint it with oil or fenugreek that has been cooked, then insert the plaster between his palms using the small spatula shown here:
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers;	 and cut the second tooth, and grind it with the nail as far as the moisture that is within the core comes out;
et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament;	 and bind the woman's belly until the child is born, and if it does not come out, you must fumigate the woman with fennel seeds and oil of lavender.
puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre:	 then make her bind herself and purge herself with cumin, hold her mouth and nose for an hour:
si istra maintenant l’enfes.	 Instructions for the thigh.
Et se les II mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc;	 If the hands come out (dislocate), you must gently pull them back a little at a time.
et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus I siege, et li lieve les piés en haut;	 and if they cannot enter (reduce), place the woman on the seat (examining table) and raise her feet.
puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement;	 then tip the chair onto the ground, and hold the woman so she does not cry out during the tilting of the chair.
et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	 if the hands cannot enter and the thigh is dead, strike the hands with the knife placed in front (of you), extract the child, and reset it equally.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piés	 Of the birth of the child upon its feet
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	 When the thigh comes above the feet, push it upwards;
et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;	 and then turn it a little at a time until it is level.
puis preigne I des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	 Then take the piece and stretch it bit by bit.
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;	 If it reaches up to the thighs, instruct him to grab hold of it, and make it vomit out of his anus.
si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	 If it goes forward, may God will it.
Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	And if it is not as we have said, turn it little by little until it is according to the natural figure.
Car adonques ist il legierement.	Therefore it should be done gently.
Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons, dit si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en I mortier;	 And if it does not go forward as we have experienced, say that he should take myrrh from above, oil of sesame, and melted gum, and grind all in a mortar.
et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement, puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;	 And put the mixture inside a woman's nature and apply this ointment externally, then make him sit in hot water up to his chest.
et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai I coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;	 And when it is softened beneath, let the collar of myrrh be placed on him, and let him rest for an hour.
puis la fai seoir sus I siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	 Then make it sit on the chair, then make it vomit and hold its mouth and nose, and press its belly gently, for the infant is about to be born now.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	Of the birth of the child on its genitals
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;	 When the baby comes in this form, put the midwife's hands little by little.
puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor I lit;	 then be supported on its neck, and let the feet hang downwards, and it lies on the bed.
et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu’elle soit appareillie aval;	 and fold its hands little by little, and then press its hands above the belly, and push the hips downwards until it is prepared for delivery.
et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains;	 if the baby does not come out, take its feet and help it come out, then push its stomach upwards, and put your hands there.
et ewe l’enfant poc et poc;	 And you pull the child little by little;
et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.	 Instruct the woman that she should take hold of herself until the baby is born.
de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	The birth of a child that comes out with one hand extended.
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	 It is necessary to devise how to return the hand:
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	 if it cannot be returned, raise the woman and walk.
s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus I lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;	 If she cannot walk, have her lie on the bed, and bend her legs.
puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;	 Then bring the belladonna that I have mentioned.
et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus I siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;	 And if she does not give birth, have her sit on the chair, then study how to return the hand;
et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	 Pull the child according to its natural shape, make her vomit, and have her hold herself until the baby is born for sure.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	Hold the baby by the neck and spread your hands apart, then turn your body towards the back of its mother.
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	 It is necessary that the barber press his hand, then turns it slowly and gently.
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	 And when they are even, he puts some muscle-relaxing substance of alum and oil (as we have said), then commands it to move slowly.
et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus I siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne;	 And when you have done this, make her sit on the chair, and command her to grab it;
et la fai esternuer.	 and make her vomit.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	in the same way, treat all similarly
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	 When the second finger comes in this manner, grab the second finger with your nail until the moisture is evacuated;
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	 and if the serpent enters on its face or neck, grab it with a rope, so that it is not held back, and kill the serpent.
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	 Then put the child inside, until you have placed it as needed, and command the woman to take hold of herself once:
adonques si istra legierement.	 then gently.
de l’issue des gemelz	From the birth of twins   (In this context, "gemelz" refers to twins, as "gele" means a twin in Old French)
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII;	 Know that twins are born often, and sometimes three or four.
et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	 and this is not an unusual occurrence, it happens.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	 Twins are rare and do not live unless named.
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	 I know that they can be increased and are deprived by the one who divides them, which is tied to the womb.
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	 and sometimes they come out naturally like a child under the mother's belly, as we have said.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	 And if they come out forcefully, the treatment is as we have said, and let the doctor be subtle, and do quickly and gently what he does.
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	 And make him do as he needs to move towards health.
de plusors enfans	Of many children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris I ou II ou III ou IIII ou V ou VI ou VII, ou plusors jusc’a XV, et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	 There are sometimes formed in the marriage between I, II, III, IV, V or VI, or up to XV, and they are all formed in the shape of a child by the measurement of his age, and it is necessary that the bailiff knows this because on occasion similar things happen.
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	 If he does as he should.
de l’enfant mort	Of a dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	 When you are curing the woman of a dead or unborn child, as I said in the division, and it does not come out forcefully, and you are forced to work by hand.
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	 If you need to know if the woman is of pure virtue, and she has no accident or fear of death.
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	 The woman must lie on her back, with her hips inclined downward, and her legs raised.
et li ministre la teigne de II pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	 And the midwife pulls it in two parts, or she is tied to the bed so that she is not treated during childbirth.
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	 Then rub the mouth of the wife with moist oil mixed with myrrh and camphor and flax seeds, then anoint the midwife's hands with these oils and these mixtures.
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere I leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu, et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	 Then push gently into the wife, then seek out the place where she pushes the child's head and make sure that it is ready for delivery.
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez, et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	 If the head is not visible, push the baby's head into the woman's womb, her neck, mouth, palate, below the beard, or in the groin or near the hips, and if the delivery is on feet, push or apply pressure to the middle of the ribs.
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	 It should be translated as: "And it is necessary that you press the anus with your right hand, and place the thumb between its two sides with the left hand, and push gently with all of your hand, and insert the thumb into one of the places that we have mentioned until it reaches the empty space.
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	 "And this is the shape of the anus:
puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	 "Then insert into the opposite anus, or if there are multiple, so that the extractions are equal.
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	 "And then stretch them equally by moving from both sides to make them come out, and the anuses should be closed to keep them shut, as shown in the figure:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	 "And if there remains any part, then the bailiff presses one of his fingers on oil and pushes it into that part, and pulls the other part.
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	 And if there remains no socket, set this bone or higher in place, and hold it until it goes completely out.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	 And if one hand comes before the other and cannot be returned due to strain, then you must wrap it up in a cloth until it goes completely out.
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	 Then break the toe at the joint or edge, and you must do the same for the other foot and both feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	 If the child's head is large and it is narrow at the exit or has a sharp point assembled, then you must insert the spinal needle between your fingers and open the sharp part and extract it.
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	 or you turn to the instrument called "almidach," from which the shape of the instruments or chapter that follows it comes.
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	 And in the same way make him (the patient) fasten himself with a large natural birth;
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	 Then draw out the bones with pliers, and if the shoulder joint jumps out and it is held by force, cut (the bone) until the moisture that is deeper issues.
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	 And if it cannot be drawn out, then break it into pieces as much as you can.
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	 And if it is swollen in the belly or beneath the ribs, it is necessary that you pierce (the area) until the moisture runs out.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the child is on its feet, the delivery is easy, and the guidance towards the mouth of the birth canal is light.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	 And if it is strained in the belly or at the groin, it must be drawn out with the hand wrapped in a cloth.
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	 And make the belly or the groin, until the moisture that is there runs out.
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	 And if the other member is dislocated and the head remains, press the ball of the hand into the socket of the joint, and pull it back to the mouth of the joint.
puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer;	 then push in once or twice, and pull harder.
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	 and if the mouth of the joint is narrowed due to an abscess that has come, do not try to force it, instead administer moist and fat things.
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	 apply plasters, and soothe with warm softening and moistening remedies.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	 If the intestines are on top of the side and can be pushed back in place, apply what was said earlier for a living child.
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	 And if it cannot be pushed back, pull it out in pieces, leaving nothing of the contents.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	 And when you have done this, present him with what we have said in abscess poultices that come for the woman's ailment;
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	 and if bleeding comes, let it be stopped by tight binding, and present other treatments.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut .i. autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	I saw a woman whose womb had been dead, then the first doctor consulted with another on this matter and revived the fetus.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time an abscess appeared in the buttock, and swelled so much that it opened up, and began to cause great pain.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was summoned to care for it, and I thought about it for a long time, but could not heal the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I placed strong plaster on it, and a bone came out, and after some days another one did.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I marveled greatly because the belly has no bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	I thought it was the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;	 I want to treat the wound, and press hard on the bones until the woman is in better condition;
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	 let her remain in this state for a long time, then add some beech bark to the place;
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	 and I have not heard of this chapter being used except when the master finds a strange thing that he knows how to help with it.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	to bring back the marriage to its place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres;	 Here comes the form of the forceps, which we use in books;
et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	 And to the shoulders turning from their joints. (In this context, "II" is Old French for "the", so the translation could also be "to the shoulders dislocating from their joints.")
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	 Furthermore, the cannula should be more delicate in constriction, and made of ebony or boxwood.
et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	 And its mouth at the end of the cannula should be wide, and the trees' bark edges should be there, and a length of one and a half palm.
et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	 And between the two joints there should be two identical cannulas from the same tube, which are closed at both ends, with a length of half a palm or a little more.
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	 And these two cannulas are inserted into the mouth of the mallet to open when turning the shoulders.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	 Another form, resembling a more subtle and lighter one, should be made of yew or boxwood, similar to the shape of pliers.
et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large;	 And let the handle and the jaws, as you see, be one palm length, and two fingers wide.
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	 And when you see opening the woman on all the equipment, let her sit on the bed, with her feet hanging and legs open, then push the two pliers together into the woman, and hold the head of the instrument underneath between her knees.
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	 Then work your hand on all the equipment, as you have done with the pliers equally, according to the amount that you see opening the mouth of the woman, until the baby does what it wants.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances;	 These things are all covered and are numerous in their similarities.
et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	 And when the mirrors have been set up, the work is more urgent, and higher for mankind due to their quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	Never leave the tool unprepared, for its necessity is not excusable.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	 When the second pouch is retained during childbirth, you must instruct the patient to hold in her anus, and then make her vomit by shaking her, and hold your hands at her mouth and nose.
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	 And if she jumps due to this, it is well.
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	 If this does not happen, take the pot, and make it a plug or a stopper, and place herbs that can open the mouth of the mare, such as rue, anise, chamomile, cascara sagrada, and centaury.
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;	 All these herbs, or some of them, are to be cooked or put in water over fire.
puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris;	 then insert a straw or tube into the pot, and put the other end into the mouth of the woman, and squeeze as much as the vapors enter inside the woman.
puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	 then make her vomit, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	If the second one jumps hastily.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;	 If she remains after this cure and does not fart, command the nurse to moist her left hand with oil of sage or mustard oil from elder, then rub it on naturally, and wait for the second time.
et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	 and when she has found it, take it and stretch it slowly, straightening it so that the woman does not shriek at the extraction.
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie;	 But it must be moved gently to the right and to the left, and then pulled out.
si venra et se desaerdra.	 Then it will come out and dislocate.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	 And if the mouth of the wound is stretched out, we have said the cure for evacuation and the fumigation of herbs.
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	 and if it is not all that we have said, ensure that you do not pull too hard.
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	 But it is necessary that the one at the mouth of the wound tie it to the woman's thigh, then clisterize with an ointment called tetrafarmaçon.
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer;	 If it will pass and be returned, it will come out stronger.
mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	 However, if it does not pass and if it brings a bad smell to the stomach and head, it burns the patient.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu:	 Therefore, it is necessary to use suitable fumigations for this:
aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	 Any of the ancients have proven fumigation of dill and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The shape of the instrument used to fumigate the woman for the retention of flowers and the second birth is as follows:    (This sentence is incomplete, so I couldn't provide a full translation)
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	 And it is to be seen like a small stone, and the head is put in its place in nature, and the arms placed over the fire.
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	 And let the fumigation be on hot coals, and the burning until it is extinguished, then start another.
de percier lou fondement	to drill the foundation
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	 Many children are born who do not have the foundation pierced, instead they have been stopped up with some subtle sifak.
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	 Therefore, in birthing, that sifak should be pierced at its proper place, not with a sharp spatula, and carefully so as not to touch the baby.
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then put a soft cloth soaked in wine and oil on it, then apply an ointment until it heals.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that it will reopen, place a leaden cannula over it (the boil), and leave it for several days, and remove it when the pus begins to move towards the rooms (of the body).
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme;	 Sometimes there comes this stopping of sudden pain from a wound or abscess.
si covient coper celui soudement:	 it is necessary to cover that sudden pain:
si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	 if it can be healed as we have said from the juice of walnuts.
de la fistule dou fondement	of the fistula from the foundation
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;	 Fistulas that come from under the foundation are swelling, and those that come above the foundation discharge fluid or pus, or in the space between two parts, if there is one fistula or several.
et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans;	 and when that swelling has been present for a long time, it becomes hard, and sometimes moisture causes a boil or a thin abscess, and at times these fistulas are persistent.
et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	 And are known by those who understand that it is either an evacuation or windiness when the patient makes an evacuation, and possibly a jump from one side to another.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge;	 If the ulcers that pierce until the bladder, and up to half the penis;
et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	 reach the joint of the calf, and the knee bone.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	 And thus one recognizes a persistent ulcer at its base, and not a persistent one:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	 And you shall press your thumb or base onto the ulcer, and insert a fine needle of iron or bronze into the ulcer where there is no twisting.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	 If it has a twisting, then insert a thin reed or horsehair until you feel the reed or hair on your thumb.
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	 And if you do not feel it (the dislocation), it will not cause death, nor pus, nor wind, as we have said.
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie;	 know that it does not pierce (through)
si te haste dou curer.	 hurry up to heal (it).
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula has perforated up to the bladder or up to the conduit of urine, if it spouts urine and cannot heal with medicines.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	 If it pierces up to the knee-joint, then the tendon comes up to the level.
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	 if there is no twisting and the pain around it, then it remains (in place) bent and does not require medicine or treatment with salves.
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	 And in these Persian fistulas, there is no remedy but labor, and the vanity of foolish healers who meddle with them.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos;	 In those which are not Persian and not ancient, there is hope for healing by iron, as I have experienced, and the patient lies between your hands on his back.
et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	 And bend the legs up to the thighs, and have the thighs inclined towards the belly;
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	 Then insert an arrow tent or a plank if there is curvature, as long as you know where the dislocation comes from.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet;	 If the patient feels it around the base, you must insert your index finger, then if it sinks in, you know that the arrow has pierced.
et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	 and uncovered or you feel between your finger the shaft or the meat, then you know it has penetrated.
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	 if not worked at all, it cannot be healed.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	 It is said that some can be well healed, but this happens little;
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	 and the help is what is done, it is heating the cautery fine according to the width of the wound, as previously said.
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement;	 And push everything hot into the fistula until it comes out of its base.
et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	 And do this two or three times until you know that these charred items are burned, which resemble a bird feather.
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	 And then heal it with moistened tents in butter until the burn heals, then heal it with a healing ointment that burns and seals.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	 If it is thus healed, it is good.
Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	 If this cannot be healed otherwise;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	 and if the tent enters but does not penetrate to the base, place a thick layer of charcoal or silk between your hand and the tent, so that you can see the fistula through this cover of charcoal or silk.
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	 if the head of the fistula starts at its beginning, push the tent forward and then burn it up to the tip of the tent.
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra;	 And the tenter and sheriff will be delivered.
puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	 Then bind those charred limbs that appear like a bird's feather, leaving nothing behind.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the wound gapes and separates, cut between you and it, then cauterize with fire or medicine ointment.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses:	 For the fire cautery brings together two good things:
c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	 It is to know, the scalding of these charred things, and the stopping of blood and the drying of moisture.
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	 then the treatment of damp tents with butter or boiled cheese until the wound heals over, and when the flesh has grown enough, the burnt things should be put in the wound.
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	 then treat the wound with onions boiled in strong charcoal and dry medicine.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is restored, it becomes healed and does not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	If a fistula comes all the way up to the bottom, and is separated from the body, push your thumb or finger against the bottom, and check it.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre II est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des III manieres:	 If you feel the wound and there is cloth or linen or burnt things between it close to being pierced, have no fear as long as there is a way of faith and hope through one of the three methods:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	 or you can cauterize it as we have said, or you pierce it to the bottom, or if there is pus you put fresh tents on and treat it as before.
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	 And go not too deep, so that you cover the holding device for the foundation, and the evacuations come through by voluntary sensation.
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	 Then heal, as we have said.
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	 If by chance it will be healed, then remove that covering and wash it when it is cut away from the foundation, either by a tent or any other instrument pointed.
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	 Then disinfect the flesh graft in the wound as much as you can.
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement:	 Then study to restore the wound, and to keep the fistula on the side opposite the foundation.
si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	 If it will be easier for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere:	 And sometimes fistulas are as follows:
et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus, si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	 and when you pull the tent in the fistula and it is on the side of the foundation under the skin above, then take a perforated tent at the top in this manner:
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	and insert one thread twisted in two, and press the tent on the entire length of the thread into the fistula until it reaches the head (or top).
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	 If it is perforated on the edge of the foundation within, then draw out the thread of the perforation, thus you push your finger or foundation.
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les II chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse I jor ou II;	 and draw out the head of the thread, and bring together the two shoulders and hold one against the other, and leave it for a day or two.
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	 and keep it immobile until the threads heal the charred area and heal.
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	 Then treat the wound until it is healed and healthy.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not pierce through, make it pierce in all possible ways, if it is not too deep.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	It is not advisable to treat a dislocated joint by covering it tightly and then curing it while it is still unhealthy.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	 The shape of the spurred spear-point from which a fistula is made is very sharp on one side and cuts through.
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	 and on the other side it is not sharp, so that one does not cut what one should not cut, as you can see here.
des emorroydes	piles (hemorrhoids)
Emorrydes sont selonc II manieres:	 Emorydes are of two kinds:
ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc, et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement;	 or they are within the foundation, as with resin grains, and there are small and large ones, and on the outside there is blood, and there may be one or more, and they turn away from the foundation and toward the top of the foundation:
mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor, et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	 but those that turn away have a little moisture, and there is either a little lemon juice or a little blood, and they have the color of the body:
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	 and the treatment for those within the foundation, is that you instruct the patient to strain himself to urinate in a chamber until the foundation dissolves, and this appears as thread-like material:
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	 if you hurry, and it is with tweezers or you hold it with your nail, then break it at its roots.
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a I drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	 And if the finger cannot be held due to moisture, take it with linen cloth or cotton, or a piece of chamois leather.
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	 Then pull them apart, then strike them, and powder some hot powders on top, instead of a fire cautery.
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, pues les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	 Or cauterize them as said in the chapter on cautery, then treat with other remedies until they are healed.
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	 If the underlying cause cannot be drawn out, then clisterize the patient with biting and harsh clisteria to clean the area where the underlying cause is, so that it can come out openly.
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	 When the patient washes himself, and if the threads are forced from the abscess, then the treatment is easy.
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	 And it is that you seize them with your nail or tongs, and strike them, then heal them as we have said, until they are healed, and fear the incision by iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere:	 It must be done thus: bring forth the stitching...
pren I fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les II chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille, et si soit dou large;	 Take the twisted thread and put it in a needle, then pull the thread above and pierce the needle from the other side, and turn both ends of the thread under the needle, making it large.
et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse I por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	 And form a knot, then knot the thread, and draw out the needle, and do this with all the others, and leave a space for the blood to flow.
puis met sus le fondement I drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	 Then put the damp cloth soaked in rose oil or pitch on top of the foundation, and place it there, and instruct the patient to rest.
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And then let it drain until it stops, and when it has stopped, you should treat it with ointment and other treatment, until it heals.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	The dry heat of the fire or foundation
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Often, there is dryness from fever in the intestines, and due to the natural constraint, when the sickness is old and medicine has no effect.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	 You must scrape the skin's surface with a small metal tool or nail to prevent it from becoming moist.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	 then treat it until it is healed as required.
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	 If it cannot heal, then repeat the scraping more forcefully than before, until it heals completely and the skin is removed.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then treat it until it is healed.
dou fremit	toothache
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	 A frog-like growth that appears on the body, and moves a lot.
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	 Sometimes it is difficult to distinguish between the frogs and the tumors, they feel like deathly cold and come all over the body, more in the hands than in other parts.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	 And the remedy is that you take a cane from an goose quill or a strong eagle feather, and put that cane on the trembling, until the purple circles surround the trembling completely.
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	 Then turn your hand along the entire cane so that you cover all of the trembling, and immerse it completely, and harden the trembling from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you see, do as with a cat's incision of honey or iron according to this form, and be subtle beneath and draw above.
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser.	 Do not pierce, but rather press with your fingers.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	 And if you wish, you can cauterize the trembling as described in the chapter on cautery.
de la forme dou clistere	of the form of the clyster   (enema)
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet;	 Sometimes a silver or pitch clyster is made, or melted beeswax or honey.
et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	 And sometimes these small and large instruments are made according to those who need them.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Therefore, when treating children who are weak and painful, they are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The shape of the cucurbit is both small and large, or the belly is tied in this manner:   (Note that "cucurbit" was incorrectly provided instead of "clistere".)
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez;	 And it shall have an opening where the belly is tied, as you see, and the head pierced within.
et ait a l’un des costez II pertus, et en l’autre I;	 And on one side it shall be pierced twice, and in the other one.
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus, et ait entre chescun pertus I doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus I fil fort de fil crut tort en X ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	 And the belly or stomach should be filled with medicines from a beast's bladder or parchment, and it shall be pierced all around with small holes, and there should be space between each hole, then insert strong thread of twisted thread through each hole, X or Y number around, and bind the stomach as if it is a sheep's purse.
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize;	 And when the medicines are inside, tie it with strong thread to the instrument in front, then cleanse.
et c’est li forme dou cercle:	 This is the form of a circle:
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	 And let the medicine not be too hot or too cold, and anoint the head with linseed oil or egg yolk, or something similar, then gently apply it.
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses II mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit, et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet;	 Then the attendants should separate the patient's legs with their two hands, as much as they can see, then remove the linseed oil or egg yolk, and wash the patient's legs in public. If the medicine appears, apply it as much as possible.
et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	 And if he sleeps all night, it is a greater help.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you plaster the patient with belly distention caused by gas, and the medicine appears to work quickly, continue until he is healed.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por I enfant;	 If the hemorrhoids are festered or abscessed, let the linseed oil be as fine as for a child.
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	 And this is the form of the fine linseed oil where the skin is stretched:
des plaies	in the treatment of wounds;
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies;	 We have already said in the division the treatment of wounds;
or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	 We will tell you about the treatments for hands and medicine, according to completion.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are diverse according to what they are made of, and according to the places where the wounds are made, and how they are made.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	 The things by which wounds are made are by the thrust of a sword, the cut of a knife or a lance or a staff or an arrow or similar things;
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	 or which are made according to the laws of the body, such as a wound that falls on the neck, or the head, or the chest, or the stomach, or the liver, and similar limbs;
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	 and I will tell you the treatment for each wound, and I will begin with the simple wounds of the head, for memory will come in its chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans, et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut:	 I say that when a simple wound or head comes about and the bone is not broken, be careful if it is due to an arrow or similar things, and the skin is completely torn and the wound is large, and you doubt the abscess has formed deeply:
si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	 treat it with hot oil immediately if the wound is shallow and there is little blood from the wound, and apply the hot oil to the opposite side of the injured part.
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	 empty the patient's fullness of wine and heavy foods.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	 And if it does not want to heal, reduce its food, do not drink wine, and do not eat meat.
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	 and place on the wound if an abscess comes up, cotton dampened in rose oil only or in stypic wine.
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	 And if there is no abscess heated, place it on the wound, if it is fresh with all its blood, and it is not moved by air or powder, I will say a little more about it afterwards;
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And if the arteries have moved it, place some remedies on it until it heals.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	And if the wound is large like a sword and similar, and the lips cannot be brought together by sutures, bring them together by sewing, as I shall say for the abdominal wounds, with suturing.
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope;	 If the wound is exposed to the bone, and hollow, and does not hold together but only slightly, bind it.
puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir, et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	 Then cure the wound with medicine, use tough leather instead of skin, and instruct the patient to eat thick foods such as cooked tests (head) and wheat, also asparagus, and similar things.
