et estendent amont et aval tuit a une fois, tant que li malaide soit levez de terre a une fois, et demoure pendans.	 And they stretch upwards and downwards all at once, as long as the patient is raised from the ground only once, and remains hanging there.
Ceste maniere d’estension si est commune as .iiij. semblances, et se li dislocation est revenue, si com nos avons dit, c’est bien.	This way of extension is common to the four similar cases, and if the dislocation returns, as we have said, it is good.
Se ceu non, si covient mettre cure a sa semblance.	 If that does not happen, then you must give treatment for its similar symptoms.
Quant li dislocations est au pardedens, si covient que tu sovines le malaide sus son costeit sain, puis met le liien sus la racine de la cuixe, et le leu qui est desoz l’angre, puis estent le liien en haut devers l’angre, et devers la forcele;	 When the dislocation is at the shoulder joint, you must hold the patient on their healthy side, then place the rope around the root of the thigh, and the limb that is under the angle (arm pit), then pull the rope upwards towards the angle, and towards the elbow.
puis preigne uns autres ministres ses bras, et embraice le gros leu de la cuixe malaide, et l’estende au defuer forment:	 Then take another minister (helper) by their arms, and embrace the diseased thigh's large part, extending it in a wide manner.
si revenra a son leu maintenant;	 It will return to its place now.
et ceste maniere de dislocation est plus legiere des autres.	 And this kind of dislocation is easier than others.
Et se tu ne la pues serrer en ceste maniere que nos avons dit, si covient que tu lies les II piés dou malaide ensamble d’un fort liien souef sus les II talons, et sus les II genous, et soit li jambe malaide estendue II dois plus que li autres;	 If you cannot hold it in this manner as we have said, then you must tie the two feet of the patient together with a strong rope above the heels and knees, and the injured leg should be extended two fingers' breadth more than the other.
puis soit pendus sus le chief d’un fust, et soit en sus de terre II bras de lonc;	 Then it should be suspended from above with a beam, and there should be two arms' length between it and the ground.
puis comande a I ministre qu’il embraice le chief de la cuixe, et soit uns autres ministres pendans avec le malaide, qui embraice forment la cuixe, car li jointure revient maintenant hastanment.	 Then instruct the assistant to grasp the thigh and another assistant should be hanging with the patient, who grasps the thigh firmly, as the joint will return quickly now.
Et quant li dislocations est au defuer, si gise li malaides, si com nos avons dit en celui qui a gilbositeit, et estraigne I liien sus la jambe malaide proprement, et sus le peis ausi;	 And when the dislocation is facing away, let the patient lie as we have said in the case of one who has gout, and pull the rope up over the injured leg properly, and also over the thigh.
puis met II tisons, I au chief et I autre as piez, puis fiche I tison entre les cuixes au malaide emmi la forme;	 Then put two hot iron rods, one at the head and another at the feet, then insert the iron rod between the thighs of the patient in the shape.
et ait plantei de drapelz moistes entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide, puis estende chescuns ministre devers lui, et li mires mette igal a sa main la dislocation.	 and plant damp cloths around it so that it does not blister the patient, then each minister extends towards him, and the mirror puts his hand equal to the dislocation.
S’elle revient, c’est boin.	 If it comes back, that is good.
Se ce non, met sus .ie. table, et le presse ensi com nos avons dit en la gilbositeit, et gise li malaides sus le sain costeit.	 If it does not come back, place him on a table and press as we have said in the case of gout, and make the patient lie on the healthy side.
Et quant li dislocations est devant, si covient estendre la jambe malaide hastanment, et selonc ce que j’ai dit;	 And when the dislocation is in front, it is necessary to stretch the sick leg immediately, and as I have said;
et mette li mires sa paine d’estre sus l’angre malaide, puis presse a l’autre main, et l’estent aval devers lou genoil.	 and the mirror places his pain on top of the angry dislocation, then presses with the other hand, and stretches it down towards the knee.
Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les II hainches;	 And if the dislocation is to the rear, it should not be stretched down, nor lifted up from the ground, but it should remain as when a horse's harness is dislocated to the rear, as we have said in the lying down on two horses.
et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table;	 And it (the affected body part) should be placed on its side (or flat), and the limb stretched out as we have said before, and it must be pressed against the joint on a solid surface.
et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz;	 And the patient will extend their legs, and they should be even (level).
adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve;	 Then adjust the thighs, place the affected leg, and tie it with a bandage so that the affected limb does not move.
et se repose III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus;	 And rest for three or four days, then untie it, and place the affected leg again.
et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse III jors;	 If you see that they are level (equal), tie it as before, and let it rest for three days.
puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	 Then untie it, and make the patient walk slowly, until the limb is comfortable.
de la dislocation dou genoil	Of the dislocation of the knee
Li genous est desaluez selonc III manieres:	 The genou (knee) can become dislocated in three ways:
c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier;	 that is to say, internally and externally, and backwards.
et ne desalue point devant.	 it does not dislocate forward.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez;	 And the signs are that you instruct the patient to bend his leg at the knee, and if it does not bend at the knee, then you know that it is dislocated.
et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez;	 and the restoration of all (the dislocations) is that you make the patient sit straight, extend his leg if he can, and place your back on his front, and place his foot on your feet.
puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les II costez dou genoil forment;	 then take hold of the knee with both hands, pull it straight between your hands, and bend the two sides of the knee outwardly.
et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement;	 And another servant extends his foot until the knee returns to its place, and the sign is that he bends his leg gently at the knee.
et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie;	 Then apply the plaster, and hold the leg bent at the knee for three or four days, then release it.
et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	 Do not move the patient, let the limbs be comforted.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	 And if the limb is not present, administer strong extension, as we have said in the treatment of the hernia, until it is healthy.
de la dislocation dou talon	of the ankle dislocation
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The heels are sometimes swollen, and sometimes completely dislocated, both inside and out.
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee:	 The sign is that the ankle is swollen and it protrudes in the direction where it has been dislocated.
li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	 The corrections are light, and they must be stretched gently to their hands when they are merely swollen.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville;	 And if it is dislocated completely, you must make the patient sit upright and hold the servant only by the leg above the ankle.
puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut;	 Then take the foot towards you with your right hand, then with your left hand twice, then lift it up and push the foot up strongly.
et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet;	 And do this twice as we have said, pushing and pulling the foot.
s’elle revient, c’est bien;	 if it returns, that is good;
se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient;	 if not, then repeat the work, because it will return.
et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide;	 and if it cannot return like that, make the patient lie on his back on the ground, and insert the probe firmly into the ground between his legs, and tie strips around it so as not to cut the patient.
puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet;	 then the attendants mark the leg, and another attendant extends the foot to his hands or to the chain, so that it lies on the neck of the foot.
puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent;	 Then extend each instrument equally, and place the patient's legs together close to the patient so as to hold the patient while stretching.
puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	 Then grab the dislocated joint with both hands, and another instrument hold the healthy leg below it, and the dislocation will return quickly.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois;	 And when it is in place, put the padding and muffler on top of it, hold it in position with force, tie the foot to the healthy leg, and watch the nerves that are above the back of the ankle, so the bindings are not too tight.
puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain;	 Then leave it for two or three days, and if the bindings loosen, tighten them again.
puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors;	 Untie it on the third day or the fourth, and have the patient walk for four days.
et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	 And if it goes towards that point, it is not certain that it will not dislocate again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if an abscess swells up, you must treat it as we have said elsewhere, until it is healthy.
des dois	The two [things] (or parts)
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When the two [things] are dislocated, they must be stretched gently without strain, and it is an easy task.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne;	 If the dislocation is on any side of the back or hip, you must make the patient sit upright on a flat surface such as a bed or table, and put your foot on the affected joint opening. Then press firmly with your foot until it returns to its place.
et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie;	 And when it is level and there is no opening, put a table under the foot of the shoulder, then press firmly, and leave it for three days, then release.
et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Let it rest until it heals.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	of wounds and dislocations together
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert:	 When a wound comes with dislocation and it is treated, many times the patient dies.
si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis;	 If you are not presumptuous in the care, if you are not skilled in the art and have not used it for a long time, and if you are not compassionate and merciful and slow, do not be hasty.
et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit;	 Use at first the cooling of an abscess hot, and leave the patient in God's hands if you see no hope of health.
et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne;	 And when you see hope, then reset the limb to its place, as long as the abscess grows warm.
et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis;	 And when the limb is in its place, then apply cooling things to the abscess, and treat the wound as needed with dry unguents.
et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples;	 And if there is a break in the dislocation and small bones dislocated, then set them, and do as we have said in simple diseases.
et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	 And keep away from entering into fear, as I have said, for this will be harmful to you according to your Creator, and because of the wisdom of your weapon and body.
